# app\api\auth\[...nextauth]\route.ts

```ts
import NextAuth from "next-auth"; import GoogleProvider from "next-auth/providers/google"; import { PrismaAdapter } from "@auth/prisma-adapter"; import { prisma } from "lib/prisma"; import { Adapter } from "next-auth/adapters"; const handler = NextAuth({ adapter: PrismaAdapter(prisma) as Adapter, providers: [ GoogleProvider({ clientId: process.env.GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID ?? "", clientSecret: process.env.GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET ?? "", allowDangerousEmailAccountLinking: true, }), ], session: { strategy: "jwt" }, pages: { signIn: '/auth/signin', error: '/error', }, callbacks: { async session({ session, token }) { if (session.user) { session.user.id = token.sub!; } return session; }, async jwt({ token, user }) { if (user) { token.id = user.id; } return token; } } }); export { handler as GET, handler as POST };
```

# app\api\auth\signin\page.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import { useEffect } from 'react'; import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation'; import { useSession, signIn } from 'next-auth/react'; export default function SignInRedirect() { const { status } = useSession(); const router = useRouter(); useEffect(() => { console.log('Sign-in page loaded.'); if (status === 'authenticated') { console.log('User already authenticated, redirecting to /dashboard.'); router.push('/dashboard'); } else if (status === 'unauthenticated') { console.log('User not authenticated, triggering Google sign-in.'); signIn('google', { callbackUrl: '/dashboard' }) .then(() => console.log('Sign-in initiated successfully.')) .catch((error) => { console.error('Sign-in error:', error); router.push('/error'); }); } }, [status, router]); return ( <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-gray-100"> <p className="text-gray-700"> {status === 'loading' ? 'Loading...' : 'Redirecting to Google sign-in...'} </p> </div> ); }
```

# app\api\meetings\[id]\export\route.ts

```ts
import { NextResponse } from 'next/server'; import { prisma } from 'lib/prisma'; import { Document, Packer, Paragraph, TextRun } from 'docx'; import type { Meeting, MeetingWithParsedFields, MeetingBreakdown, TranscriptSegment } from 'types/global'; export const GET = async ( request: Request, { params }: { params: { id: string } } ) => { const { id } = params; // Handle CORS if (request.method === 'OPTIONS') { return new Response(null, { headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*', 'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET,OPTIONS', 'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type', }, }); } try { const meeting = await prisma.meeting.findUnique({ where: { id }, include: { tasks: true, decisions: true, questions: true, insights: true, deadlines: true, attendees: true, followUps: true, risks: true, agenda: true, }, }) as unknown as Meeting; if (!meeting) { return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Meeting not found.' }, { status: 404 }); } // Parse the raw transcript to get text and segments let transcriptText = ''; let segments: TranscriptSegment[] = []; try { if (meeting.rawTranscript) { const parsed = JSON.parse(meeting.rawTranscript); transcriptText = parsed.text || meeting.rawTranscript; if (parsed.segments && Array.isArray(parsed.segments)) { segments = parsed.segments.map((segment: any) => ({ text: segment.text.trim(), start: parseFloat(segment.start), end: parseFloat(segment.end), speaker: segment.speaker || '', words: segment.words || [] })); } } } catch (e) { console.error('Failed to parse transcript:', e); transcriptText = meeting.rawTranscript || ''; } // Create the breakdown object const breakdown: MeetingBreakdown = { Tasks: meeting.tasks.map((task) => ({ task: task.task, owner: task.owner, due_date: task.dueDate, })), Decisions: meeting.decisions.map((decision) => ({ decision: decision.decision, date: decision.date, })), Questions: meeting.questions.map((question) => ({ question: question.question, status: question.status, answer: question.answer || null, })), Insights: meeting.insights.map((insight) => ({ insight: insight.insight, reference: insight.reference, })), Deadlines: meeting.deadlines.map((deadline) => ({ description: deadline.description, due_date: deadline.dueDate, })), Attendees: meeting.attendees.map((attendee) => ({ name: attendee.name, role: attendee.role, })), "Follow-ups": meeting.followUps.map((followUp) => ({ description: followUp.description, owner: followUp.owner, })), Risks: meeting.risks.map((risk) => ({ risk: risk.risk, impact: risk.impact, })), Agenda: meeting.agenda.map((item) => ({ item: item.item, })), }; // Parse JSON fields const processedMeeting: MeetingWithParsedFields = { ...meeting, segments, wordTimings: meeting.wordTimings ? JSON.parse(meeting.wordTimings) : null, speakerLabels: meeting.speakerLabels ? JSON.parse(meeting.speakerLabels) : null, breakdown, }; // Create the document const doc = new Document({ sections: [ { properties: {}, children: [ // Title new Paragraph({ text: processedMeeting.name, heading: 'Heading1', spacing: { after: 200 }, }), // Description new Paragraph({ text: 'Description', heading: 'Heading2', spacing: { before: 300, after: 200 }, }), new Paragraph({ children: [new TextRun({ text: processedMeeting.description, break: 1 })], spacing: { after: 200 }, }), // Summary new Paragraph({ text: 'Summary', heading: 'Heading2', spacing: { before: 300, after: 200 }, }), new Paragraph({ children: [new TextRun({ text: processedMeeting.summary, break: 1 })], spacing: { after: 200 }, }), // Tasks new Paragraph({ text: 'Tasks', heading: 'Heading2', spacing: { before: 300, after: 200 }, }), ...processedMeeting.tasks.map( (task) => new Paragraph({ children: [ new TextRun({ text: `Task: ${task.task}\nOwner: ${task.owner}\nDue Date: ${ task.dueDate ? new Date(task.dueDate).toLocaleDateString() : 'Not set' }\nStatus: ${task.status || 'Not set'}\n`, break: 1, }), ], spacing: { after: 200 }, }) ), // Decisions new Paragraph({ text: 'Decisions', heading: 'Heading2', spacing: { before: 300, after: 200 }, }), ...processedMeeting.decisions.map( (decision) => new Paragraph({ children: [ new TextRun({ text: `Decision: ${decision.decision}\nDate: ${new Date( decision.date ).toLocaleDateString()}\n`, break: 1, }), ], spacing: { after: 200 }, }) ), // Questions new Paragraph({ text: 'Questions', heading: 'Heading2', spacing: { before: 300, after: 200 }, }), ...processedMeeting.questions.map( (question) => new Paragraph({ children: [ new TextRun({ text: `Question: ${question.question}\nStatus: ${ question.status }\nAnswer: ${question.answer || 'Not answered'}\n`, break: 1, }), ], spacing: { after: 200 }, }) ), // Insights new Paragraph({ text: 'Insights', heading: 'Heading2', spacing: { before: 300, after: 200 }, }), ...processedMeeting.insights.map( (insight) => new Paragraph({ children: [ new TextRun({ text: `${insight.insight}\nReference: ${insight.reference}\n`, break: 1, }), ], spacing: { after: 200 }, }) ), // Deadlines new Paragraph({ text: 'Deadlines', heading: 'Heading2', spacing: { before: 300, after: 200 }, }), ...processedMeeting.deadlines.map( (deadline) => new Paragraph({ children: [ new TextRun({ text: `Description: ${deadline.description}\nDue Date: ${ deadline.dueDate ? new Date(deadline.dueDate).toLocaleDateString() : 'Not set' }\n`, break: 1, }), ], spacing: { after: 200 }, }) ), // Attendees new Paragraph({ text: 'Attendees', heading: 'Heading2', spacing: { before: 300, after: 200 }, }), ...processedMeeting.attendees.map( (attendee) => new Paragraph({ children: [ new TextRun({ text: `${attendee.name} (${attendee.role})\n`, break: 1, }), ], spacing: { after: 200 }, }) ), // Follow-ups new Paragraph({ text: 'Follow-ups', heading: 'Heading2', spacing: { before: 300, after: 200 }, }), ...processedMeeting.followUps.map( (followUp) => new Paragraph({ children: [ new TextRun({ text: `Description: ${followUp.description}\nOwner: ${followUp.owner}\n`, break: 1, }), ], spacing: { after: 200 }, }) ), // Risks new Paragraph({ text: 'Risks', heading: 'Heading2', spacing: { before: 300, after: 200 }, }), ...processedMeeting.risks.map( (risk) => new Paragraph({ children: [ new TextRun({ text: `Risk: ${risk.risk}\nImpact: ${risk.impact}\n`, break: 1, }), ], spacing: { after: 200 }, }) ), // Agenda new Paragraph({ text: 'Agenda', heading: 'Heading2', spacing: { before: 300, after: 200 }, }), ...processedMeeting.agenda.map( (item) => new Paragraph({ children: [new TextRun({ text: `• ${item.item}`, break: 1 })], spacing: { after: 100 }, }) ), // Raw Transcript new Paragraph({ text: 'Full Transcript', heading: 'Heading2', spacing: { before: 300, after: 200 }, }), new Paragraph({ children: [new TextRun({ text: transcriptText, break: 1 })], spacing: { after: 200 }, }), ], }, ], }); const buffer = await Packer.toBuffer(doc); const fileName = `${processedMeeting.name.replace(/\s+/g, '_')}_Details.docx`; return new NextResponse(buffer, { status: 200, headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document', 'Content-Disposition': `attachment; filename="${fileName}"`, }, }); } catch (error: any) { console.error(error); return NextResponse.json( { error: 'Failed to export meeting details.' }, { status: 500 } ); } };
```

# app\api\meetings\[id]\route.ts

```ts
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'; import { prisma } from 'lib/prisma'; import type { Meeting, Task, Decision, Question, Insight, Deadline, Attendee, FollowUp, Risk, AgendaItem, MeetingWithParsedFields, MeetingBreakdown, WordTiming, TranscriptSegment } from 'types/global'; // Include all fields from Meeting plus the relations type MeetingWithRelations = Meeting & { tasks: Task[]; decisions: Decision[]; questions: Question[]; insights: Insight[]; deadlines: Deadline[]; attendees: Attendee[]; followUps: FollowUp[]; risks: Risk[]; agenda: AgendaItem[]; }; const parseWordTimings = (wordTimingsStr: string | null): WordTiming[] | null => { if (!wordTimingsStr) { console.log('No word timings string provided'); return null; } try { const parsed = JSON.parse(wordTimingsStr); // Validate the parsed data structure if (!Array.isArray(parsed)) { console.error('Word timings is not an array:', typeof parsed); return null; } // Validate each word timing object const validWordTimings = parsed.filter((timing: unknown): timing is WordTiming => { if (!timing || typeof timing !== 'object') { return false; } const t = timing as any; const isValid = typeof t.word === 'string' && typeof t.start === 'number' && typeof t.end === 'number'; if (!isValid) { console.error('Invalid word timing object:', timing); } return isValid; }); console.log('Word timings parsed:', { original: parsed.length, valid: validWordTimings.length, sample: validWordTimings.slice(0, 3) }); return validWordTimings; } catch (error) { console.error('Failed to parse word timings:', error); return null; } }; const createSegmentsFromWords = (wordTimings: WordTiming[]): TranscriptSegment[] => { const segments: TranscriptSegment[] = []; let currentSegment: TranscriptSegment = { text: '', start: 0, end: 0, speaker: '', words: [] }; let words: WordTiming[] = []; wordTimings.forEach((timing, index) => { const word = timing.word.trim(); const isPunctuation = /[.!?]$/.test(word); words.push(timing); if (index === 0) { currentSegment.start = timing.start; } if (isPunctuation || index === wordTimings.length - 1) { currentSegment.text = words.map(w => w.word).join(' '); currentSegment.end = timing.end; currentSegment.words = words; segments.push({ ...currentSegment }); // Reset for next segment currentSegment = { text: '', start: timing.end, end: 0, speaker: '', words: [] }; words = []; } }); return segments; }; const parseTranscriptSegments = (rawTranscript: string | null, wordTimingsStr: string | null): TranscriptSegment[] | null => { if (!rawTranscript) { console.log('No raw transcript provided'); return null; } try { const parsed = JSON.parse(rawTranscript); // First try to get segments from raw transcript if (parsed.segments && Array.isArray(parsed.segments)) { const validSegments = parsed.segments.filter((segment: unknown): segment is TranscriptSegment => { if (!segment || typeof segment !== 'object') { return false; } const s = segment as any; const isValid = typeof s.text === 'string' && typeof s.start === 'number' && typeof s.end === 'number' && Array.isArray(s.words); if (!isValid) { console.error('Invalid segment object:', segment); } return isValid; }); if (validSegments.length > 0) { console.log('Using segments from raw transcript:', { count: validSegments.length, sample: validSegments.slice(0, 3) }); return validSegments; } } // If no segments found, try to create them from word timings console.log('No segments found in raw transcript, creating from word timings'); const wordTimings = parseWordTimings(wordTimingsStr); if (wordTimings) { const segments = createSegmentsFromWords(wordTimings); console.log('Created segments from word timings:', { count: segments.length, sample: segments.slice(0, 3) }); return segments; } return null; } catch (error) { console.error('Failed to parse segments:', error); return null; } }; export const GET = async ( request: NextRequest, { params }: { params: { id: string } } ) => { const { id } = params; try { console.log('Fetching meeting:', id); const meeting = await prisma.meeting.findUnique({ where: { id, }, include: { tasks: true, decisions: true, questions: true, insights: true, deadlines: true, attendees: true, followUps: true, risks: true, agenda: true, }, }) as MeetingWithRelations | null; if (!meeting) { return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Meeting not found.' }, { status: 404 }); } console.log('Meeting found, processing transcript data'); const segments = parseTranscriptSegments(meeting.rawTranscript, meeting.wordTimings); const wordTimings = parseWordTimings(meeting.wordTimings); console.log('Transcript data processed:', { hasSegments: !!segments, segmentsCount: segments?.length, hasWordTimings: !!wordTimings, wordTimingsCount: wordTimings?.length }); const breakdown: MeetingBreakdown = { Tasks: meeting.tasks.map((task) => ({ task: task.task, owner: task.owner, due_date: task.dueDate, })), Decisions: meeting.decisions.map((decision) => ({ decision: decision.decision, date: decision.date, })), Questions: meeting.questions.map((question) => ({ question: question.question, status: question.status, answer: question.answer || null, })), Insights: meeting.insights.map((insight) => ({ insight: insight.insight, reference: insight.reference, })), Deadlines: meeting.deadlines.map((deadline) => ({ description: deadline.description, due_date: deadline.dueDate, })), Attendees: meeting.attendees.map((attendee) => ({ name: attendee.name, role: attendee.role, })), "Follow-ups": meeting.followUps.map((followUp) => ({ description: followUp.description, owner: followUp.owner, })), Risks: meeting.risks.map((risk) => ({ risk: risk.risk, impact: risk.impact, })), Agenda: meeting.agenda.map((item) => ({ item: item.item, })), }; const processedMeeting: MeetingWithParsedFields = { ...meeting, segments, wordTimings, speakerLabels: meeting.speakerLabels ? JSON.parse(meeting.speakerLabels) : null, breakdown, }; return NextResponse.json(processedMeeting, { status: 200 }); } catch (error) { console.error('Failed to fetch meeting:', error); return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to fetch meeting.', details: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error) }, { status: 500 }); } }; export const DELETE = async ( request: NextRequest, { params }: { params: { id: string } } ) => { const { id } = params; try { await prisma.meeting.delete({ where: { id, }, }); return NextResponse.json({ message: 'Meeting deleted successfully.' }, { status: 200 }); } catch (error) { console.error(error); return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to delete meeting.' }, { status: 500 }); } };
```

# app\api\meetings\route.ts

```ts
import { NextResponse } from 'next/server'; import { prisma } from 'lib/prisma'; type MeetingWithRelations = NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.meeting.findFirst>>> & { tasks: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.task.findFirst>>>[]; decisions: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.decision.findFirst>>>[]; questions: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.question.findFirst>>>[]; insights: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.insight.findFirst>>>[]; deadlines: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.deadline.findFirst>>>[]; attendees: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.attendee.findFirst>>>[]; followUps: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.followUp.findFirst>>>[]; risks: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.risk.findFirst>>>[]; agenda: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.agendaItem.findFirst>>>[]; }; export const GET = async () => { try { const meetings = await prisma.meeting.findMany({ include: { tasks: true, decisions: true, questions: true, insights: true, deadlines: true, attendees: true, followUps: true, risks: true, agenda: true, }, orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' } }); const formattedMeetings = meetings.map((meeting: MeetingWithRelations) => ({ ...meeting, wordTimings: meeting.wordTimings ? JSON.parse(meeting.wordTimings) : null, speakerLabels: meeting.speakerLabels ? JSON.parse(meeting.speakerLabels) : null, breakdown: { Tasks: meeting.tasks.map((task: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.task.findFirst>>>) => ({ task: task.task, owner: task.owner, due_date: task.dueDate, })), Decisions: meeting.decisions.map((decision: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.decision.findFirst>>>) => ({ decision: decision.decision, date: decision.date, })), Questions: meeting.questions.map((question: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.question.findFirst>>>) => ({ question: question.question, status: question.status, answer: question.answer || null, })), Insights: meeting.insights.map((insight: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.insight.findFirst>>>) => ({ insight: insight.insight, reference: insight.reference, })), Deadlines: meeting.deadlines.map((deadline: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.deadline.findFirst>>>) => ({ description: deadline.description, due_date: deadline.dueDate, })), Attendees: meeting.attendees.map((attendee: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.attendee.findFirst>>>) => ({ name: attendee.name, role: attendee.role, })), "Follow-ups": meeting.followUps.map((followUp: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.followUp.findFirst>>>) => ({ description: followUp.description, owner: followUp.owner, })), Risks: meeting.risks.map((risk: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.risk.findFirst>>>) => ({ risk: risk.risk, impact: risk.impact, })), Agenda: meeting.agenda.map((item: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.agendaItem.findFirst>>>) => ({ item: item.item, })), }, })); return NextResponse.json(formattedMeetings, { status: 200 }); } catch (error: unknown) { console.error(error); return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to fetch meetings.' }, { status: 500 }); } };
```

# app\api\monitored-files\[fileName]\route.ts

```ts
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'; import fs from 'fs'; import path from 'path'; const MONITORED_FOLDER = path.join(process.cwd(), 'public', 'monitored'); export async function GET(request: NextRequest, { params }: { params: { fileName: string } }) { const fileName = params.fileName; const filePath = path.join(MONITORED_FOLDER, fileName); try { if (!fs.existsSync(filePath)) { return NextResponse.json({ error: 'File not found' }, { status: 404 }); } const fileBuffer = fs.readFileSync(filePath); const fileType = path.extname(fileName).slice(1); return new NextResponse(fileBuffer, { headers: { 'Content-Type': `audio/${fileType}`, 'Content-Disposition': `attachment; filename=${fileName}`, }, }); } catch (error) { console.error('Error reading file:', error); return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to read file' }, { status: 500 }); } }
```

# app\api\monitored-files\route.ts

```ts
import { NextResponse } from 'next/server'; import fs from 'fs'; import path from 'path'; const MONITORED_FOLDER = path.join(process.cwd(), 'public', 'monitored'); export async function GET() { try { // Ensure the monitored folder exists if (!fs.existsSync(MONITORED_FOLDER)) { fs.mkdirSync(MONITORED_FOLDER, { recursive: true }); } // Read files from the monitored folder const files = fs.readdirSync(MONITORED_FOLDER); // Get file details const fileDetails = files.map(file => { const filePath = path.join(MONITORED_FOLDER, file); const stats = fs.statSync(filePath); return { name: file, size: stats.size, lastModified: stats.mtime.toISOString() }; }); return NextResponse.json(fileDetails); } catch (error) { console.error('Error reading monitored folder:', error); return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to read monitored folder' }, { status: 500 }); } }
```

# app\api\process-document\route.ts

```ts
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'; export async function POST(request: NextRequest) { try { const formData = await request.formData(); const file = formData.get('file') as File; if (!file) { return NextResponse.json( { error: 'No file provided' }, { status: 400 } ); } // For now, we'll use a simple text extraction approach const text = await file.text(); return NextResponse.json({ text, metadata: { filename: file.name, type: file.type, size: file.size, } }); } catch (error) { console.error('Error processing document:', error); return NextResponse.json( { error: 'Failed to process document' }, { status: 500 } ); } }
```

# app\api\test-analyze\route.ts

```ts
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'; import axios from 'axios'; export async function POST(request: NextRequest) { try { const data = await request.json(); const { transcriptionText, timestamp } = data; console.log('Analysis Request Details:', { transcriptionTextLength: transcriptionText?.length, timestamp, }); if (!transcriptionText) { throw new Error('No transcription text provided'); } // Updated payload structure to match Langflow expectations const payload = { input_value: transcriptionText, output_type: "text", input_type: "text", tweaks: { "TextInput-ti2q5": { value: transcriptionText } } }; const response = await axios.post( 'http://127.0.0.1:7860/api/v1/run/463ebcca-f34e-46b4-b2ef-23f72f73ddf1', payload, { headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, params: { stream: false } } ); return NextResponse.json(response.data); } catch (error) { console.error('API Error:', error); return NextResponse.json( { error: 'An error occurred during processing.', details: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error' }, { status: 500 } ); } }
```

# app\api\test-data\route.ts

```ts
// app/api/test-data/route.ts import { NextResponse } from 'next/server'; const generateMockResponse = () => { // Mock transcription data const transcriptionData = { text: `[Your long transcript text goes here...]`, segments: [ { text: "First segment of speech", start: 0.0, end: 2.5 }, { text: "Second segment of speech", start: 2.5, end: 5.0 } ], language: "en", word_timestamps: [ { word: "First", start: 0.0, end: 0.5 }, { word: "segment", start: 0.5, end: 1.0 } ] }; // Create the full response structure return { success: true, data: { session_id: "87f99adc-2e48-4179-9f64-59526c78fb49", outputs: [ { inputs: { input_value: "message" }, outputs: [ { results: { breakdown: { text_key: "text", data: { text: JSON.stringify(transcriptionData), files: [], timestamp: "2024-11-27 21:57:30", flow_id: "87f99adc-2e48-4179-9f64-59526c78fb49" }, default_value: "", text: JSON.stringify(transcriptionData), sender: null, sender_name: null, files: [], session_id: "", timestamp: "2024-11-27 21:57:30", flow_id: "87f99adc-2e48-4179-9f64-59526c78fb49" } }, artifacts: { breakdown: { repr: JSON.stringify(transcriptionData), raw: JSON.stringify(transcriptionData), type: "text" } }, outputs: { breakdown: { message: JSON.stringify(transcriptionData), type: "text" } }, logs: { breakdown: [] }, messages: [ { message: JSON.stringify(transcriptionData), sender: "Machine", sender_name: "AI", session_id: "", component_id: "TextOutput-CCvSO", files: [], type: "text" } ], component_display_name: "Text Output", component_id: "TextOutput-CCvSO", used_frozen_result: false } ] } ] } }; }; export async function POST(request: Request) { // Simulate processing time await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2000)); return NextResponse.json(generateMockResponse()); }
```

# app\api\test-docling\process\route.ts

```ts
// app/api/process/route.ts import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'; import { spawn } from 'child_process'; export async function POST(req: NextRequest) { // Execute process on server-side try { const command = spawn('your-command', ['args']); return new Promise<Response>((resolve, reject) => { let output = ''; command.stdout.on('data', (data) => { output += data.toString(); }); command.stderr.on('data', (data) => { console.error(`Error: ${data}`); }); command.on('close', (code) => { if (code === 0) { resolve(NextResponse.json({ success: true, output })); } else { reject(NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: 'Process failed' }, { status: 500 })); } }); }); } catch (error) { return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to execute command' }, { status: 500 }); } }
```

# app\api\test-docling\route.ts

```ts
// app/api/test-docling/route.ts import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'; import { DoclingProcessor } from '@/lib/docling-processor'; import path from 'path'; import fs from 'fs'; import { writeFile } from 'fs/promises'; import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid'; export async function POST(request: NextRequest) { let filePath: string | null = null; try { const formData = await request.formData(); const file = formData.get('file') as File; if (!file) { return NextResponse.json( { error: 'No file provided' }, { status: 400 } ); } // Validate file type const fileExtension = path.extname(file.name).toLowerCase(); const allowedExtensions = ['.pdf', '.doc', '.docx', '.txt']; if (!allowedExtensions.includes(fileExtension)) { return NextResponse.json( { error: `Unsupported file type: ${fileExtension}. Supported types: ${allowedExtensions.join(', ')}` }, { status: 400 } ); } // Create uploads directory if it doesn't exist const uploadDir = path.join(process.cwd(), 'public', 'uploads'); if (!fs.existsSync(uploadDir)) { fs.mkdirSync(uploadDir, { recursive: true }); } // Generate unique filename const uniqueId = uuidv4(); const fileName = `${uniqueId}${fileExtension}`; filePath = path.join(uploadDir, fileName); // Convert file to buffer and save const bytes = await file.arrayBuffer(); const buffer = Buffer.from(bytes); await writeFile(filePath, buffer); console.log('Processing file:', { originalName: file.name, size: buffer.length, type: file.type, savedAs: filePath }); // Process the document with increased timeout const result = await DoclingProcessor.processDocument(filePath, { timeout: 300000, // 5 minutes }); if (!result.success) { console.error('Processing failed:', result.error); return NextResponse.json( { error: result.error || 'Processing failed', details: result.output }, { status: 500 } ); } return NextResponse.json({ success: true, output: result.output, processedFile: `/uploads/${fileName}`, }); } catch (error) { console.error('Document processing error:', error); return NextResponse.json( { error: 'An error occurred during processing', details: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error) }, { status: 500 } ); } finally { // Clean up the file if (filePath && fs.existsSync(filePath)) { try { fs.unlinkSync(filePath); } catch (error) { console.error('Error cleaning up file:', error); } } } }
```

# app\api\test-document\route.ts

```ts
import { NextResponse } from 'next/server'; import { DoclingProcessor, ProcessResult } from '../../../lib/docling-processor'; import path from 'path'; import { writeFile, mkdir } from 'fs/promises'; interface ProcessedOutput { text: string; metadata: { title: string; author: string; subject: string; keywords: string; pageCount: number; } } export async function POST(request: Request) { try { const formData = await request.formData(); const file = formData.get('file') as File; if (!file) { return NextResponse.json( { success: false, error: 'No file provided' }, { status: 400 } ); } // Ensure it's a PDF if (!file.name.toLowerCase().endsWith('.pdf')) { return NextResponse.json( { success: false, error: 'Only PDF files are supported' }, { status: 400 } ); } // Create uploads directory if it doesn't exist const uploadDir = path.join(process.cwd(), 'public', 'uploads'); try { await mkdir(uploadDir, { recursive: true }); } catch (error) { // Directory already exists or creation failed console.error('Error creating upload directory:', error); } // Create a safe filename with timestamp const timestamp = Date.now(); const safeFilename = `${timestamp}-${file.name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9.-]/g, '_')}`; const filePath = path.join(uploadDir, safeFilename); try { // Convert File to Buffer and save const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer(); const buffer = Buffer.from(arrayBuffer); await writeFile(filePath, buffer); // Process the document using DoclingProcessor const result: ProcessResult = await DoclingProcessor.processDocument(filePath); if (!result.success) { console.error('Processing error:', result.error); return NextResponse.json( { success: false, error: result.error }, { status: 500 } ); } // Parse the output string back to an object since DoclingProcessor stringifies it const parsedOutput = JSON.parse(result.output) as ProcessedOutput; return NextResponse.json({ success: true, text: parsedOutput.text, metadata: { ...parsedOutput.metadata, fileName: file.name, fileSize: file.size, format: 'pdf', processedAt: new Date().toISOString(), filePath: `/uploads/${safeFilename}` // relative path for client access } }); } catch (error: any) { console.error('File processing error:', error); return NextResponse.json( { success: false, error: error.message || 'Failed to process document' }, { status: 500 } ); } } catch (error: any) { console.error('Request handling error:', error); return NextResponse.json( { success: false, error: error.message || 'Failed to handle request' }, { status: 500 } ); } }
```

# app\api\test-transcribe\route.ts

```ts
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'; import axios from 'axios'; import fs from 'fs'; import path from 'path'; const UPLOADS_DIR = path.join(process.cwd(), 'public', 'uploads'); export async function POST(request: NextRequest) { let filePath = ''; try { const formData = await request.formData(); const file = formData.get('audio') as File; const type = formData.get('type') as string | null; const transcriptionText = formData.get('transcriptionText') as string; const timestamp = formData.get('timestamp') as string; // Add validation before logging if (!type) { return NextResponse.json( { error: 'Type parameter is required' }, { status: 400 } ); } console.log('Request Details:', { type, fileName: file?.name, fileSize: file?.size, transcriptionTextLength: transcriptionText?.length, timestamp }); let response; if (type === 'transcription') { if (!file) { throw new Error('No audio file provided'); } // Rest of the transcription code remains the same const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer(); const buffer = Buffer.from(arrayBuffer); if (!fs.existsSync(UPLOADS_DIR)) { fs.mkdirSync(UPLOADS_DIR, { recursive: true }); } const fileName = `${timestamp}.mp3`; filePath = path.join(UPLOADS_DIR, fileName); fs.writeFileSync(filePath, buffer); const payload = { output_type: "text", input_type: "text", tweaks: { "GroqWhisperComponent-d0YXz": { audio_file: filePath } } }; response = await axios.post( process.env.LANGFLOW_TRANSCRIPTION_URL!, payload, { headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, params: { stream: false } } ); } else if (type === 'analysis') { if (!transcriptionText) { throw new Error('No transcription text provided'); } const payload = { input_value: "message", output_type: "text", input_type: "text", tweaks: { "TextOutput-je7Wv": {}, "GroqWhisperComponent-d0YXz": { text: transcriptionText } } }; response = await axios.post( process.env.LANGFLOW_ANALYSIS_URL!, payload, { headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, params: { stream: false } } ); } else { throw new Error(`Invalid type: ${type}`); } // Cleanup file if needed if (filePath && fs.existsSync(filePath) && type === 'transcription') { try { fs.unlinkSync(filePath); console.log('🗑️ Cleaned up file:', filePath); } catch (cleanupError) { console.error('Failed to cleanup file:', cleanupError); } } return NextResponse.json(response.data); } catch (error) { console.error('API Error:', error); // Cleanup file on error if (filePath && fs.existsSync(filePath)) { try { fs.unlinkSync(filePath); console.log('🗑️ Cleaned up file:', filePath); } catch (cleanupError) { console.error('Failed to cleanup file:', cleanupError); } } return NextResponse.json( { error: 'An error occurred during processing.', details: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error' }, { status: 500 } ); } }
```

# app\api\transcribe\route.ts

```ts
import type { NextRequest } from 'next/server'; import { NextResponse } from 'next/server'; import axios from 'axios'; import fs from 'fs'; import path from 'path'; import { prisma } from 'lib/prisma'; import type { TranscriptionResponse, WordTiming, TranscriptSegment } from 'types/global'; const createSegmentsFromWords = (wordTimings: WordTiming[]): TranscriptSegment[] => { const segments: TranscriptSegment[] = []; let currentSegment: TranscriptSegment = { text: '', start: 0, end: 0, speaker: '', words: [] }; let words: WordTiming[] = []; wordTimings.forEach((timing, index) => { const word = timing.word.trim(); const isPunctuation = /[.!?]$/.test(word); words.push(timing); if (index === 0) { currentSegment.start = timing.start; } if (isPunctuation || index === wordTimings.length - 1) { currentSegment.text = words.map(w => w.word).join(' '); currentSegment.end = timing.end; currentSegment.words = words; segments.push({ ...currentSegment }); // Reset for next segment currentSegment = { text: '', start: timing.end, end: 0, speaker: '', words: [] }; words = []; } }); return segments; }; const parseTranscriptionResponse = (transcriptionResult: any) => { try { console.log('Parsing transcription result:', { hasWordTimestamps: !!transcriptionResult.word_timestamps, isArray: Array.isArray(transcriptionResult.word_timestamps), sampleTimestamp: transcriptionResult.word_timestamps?.[0] }); // Extract the word timestamps const wordTimings = transcriptionResult.word_timestamps?.map((timing: any) => ({ word: timing.word.trim(), start: parseFloat(timing.start), end: parseFloat(timing.end), confidence: timing.confidence || 1 })) || []; console.log('Parsed word timings:', { count: wordTimings.length, sample: wordTimings.slice(0, 3) }); // Create segments from word timings const segments = createSegmentsFromWords(wordTimings); console.log('Created segments:', { count: segments.length, sample: segments.slice(0, 3) }); // Create a structured response object const response = { text: transcriptionResult.text || '', segments, word_timestamps: wordTimings, language: transcriptionResult.language || 'en', duration: transcriptionResult.duration || 0 }; return response; } catch (error) { console.error('Failed to parse transcription:', error); return { text: '', segments: [], word_timestamps: [], language: 'en', duration: 0 }; } }; export const POST = async (request: NextRequest) => { let filePath = ''; try { console.log('🚀 Starting transcription process...'); const formData = await request.formData(); const file = formData.get('audio') as File; const fullPath = formData.get('fullPath') as string; console.log('📦 Received file:', { name: file?.name, size: file?.size, type: file?.type, path: fullPath }); if (!file) { console.error('❌ No audio file provided'); return NextResponse.json({ error: 'No audio file provided.' }, { status: 400 }); } // Save file const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer(); const buffer = Buffer.from(arrayBuffer); const uploadsDir = path.join(process.cwd(), 'public', 'uploads'); if (!fs.existsSync(uploadsDir)) { fs.mkdirSync(uploadsDir, { recursive: true }); } const fileName = `${Date.now()}-${file.name}`; filePath = path.join(uploadsDir, fileName); const audioFileUrl = `/uploads/${fileName}`; fs.writeFileSync(filePath, buffer); console.log('💾 File saved:', filePath); const apiUrl = process.env.LANGFLOW_FLOW_URL; if (!apiUrl) { throw new Error('LANGFLOW_FLOW_URL is not defined'); } console.log('🔄 Sending to LangFlow:', apiUrl); const payload = { output_type: 'text', input_type: 'text', tweaks: { 'GroqWhisperComponent-Y7ZzR': { audio_file: filePath, }, }, }; console.log('📤 Payload:', payload); const apiResponse = await axios.post<TranscriptionResponse>(apiUrl, payload, { headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', }, }); console.log('✅ LangFlow response received'); if (!apiResponse.data?.outputs?.[0]?.outputs) { throw new Error('Invalid API response structure'); } const outputs = apiResponse.data.outputs; const analyzedTranscript = outputs[0]?.outputs[0]?.results?.breakdown?.text; const transcriptionResult = outputs[0]?.outputs[1]?.results?.transcription; if (!analyzedTranscript || !transcriptionResult) { throw new Error('Missing transcript data'); } // Parse the transcription result const parsedTranscription = parseTranscriptionResponse(transcriptionResult); console.log('Transcription parsed:', { textLength: parsedTranscription.text.length, segmentsCount: parsedTranscription.segments.length, wordTimingsCount: parsedTranscription.word_timestamps.length, language: parsedTranscription.language, duration: parsedTranscription.duration }); let analyzedData; try { analyzedData = JSON.parse(analyzedTranscript); } catch (error) { throw new Error('Failed to parse transcript JSON'); } // Save to database const meeting = await prisma.meeting.create({ data: { name: analyzedData['Meeting Name'] || 'Untitled Meeting', description: analyzedData['Description'] || 'No description provided.', rawTranscript: parsedTranscription.text, // Store only the text summary: analyzedData['Summary'] || '', audioFile: audioFileUrl, wordTimings: JSON.stringify(parsedTranscription.word_timestamps), speakerLabels: transcriptionResult.speaker_labels ? JSON.stringify(transcriptionResult.speaker_labels) : null, confidence: 0.95, language: parsedTranscription.language, duration: parsedTranscription.duration, fileSize: buffer.length, format: path.extname(file.name).slice(1), tasks: { create: (analyzedData['Tasks'] || []) .filter((task: any) => task && typeof task === 'object') .map((task: any) => ({ task: task.task || 'No task description', owner: task.owner || 'Unassigned', dueDate: task.due_date ? new Date(task.due_date) : null, })), }, decisions: { create: (analyzedData['Decisions'] || []) .filter((decision: any) => decision && typeof decision === 'object') .map((decision: any) => ({ decision: decision.decision || 'No decision description', date: decision.date ? new Date(decision.date) : new Date(), })), }, questions: { create: (analyzedData['Questions'] || []) .filter((question: any) => question && typeof question === 'object') .map((question: any) => ({ question: question.question || 'No question', status: question.status || 'Unanswered', answer: question.answer || null, })), }, insights: { create: (analyzedData['Insights'] || []) .filter((insight: any) => insight && typeof insight === 'object') .map((insight: any) => ({ insight: insight.insight || 'No insight', reference: insight.reference || '', })), }, deadlines: { create: (analyzedData['Deadlines'] || []) .filter((deadline: any) => deadline && typeof deadline === 'object') .map((deadline: any) => ({ description: deadline.description || 'No deadline description', dueDate: deadline.date ? new Date(deadline.date) : null, })), }, attendees: { create: (analyzedData['Attendees'] || []) .filter((attendee: any) => attendee && typeof attendee === 'object') .map((attendee: any) => ({ name: attendee.name || 'Unnamed Attendee', role: attendee.role || 'No role specified', })), }, followUps: { create: (analyzedData['Follow-ups'] || []) .filter((followUp: any) => followUp && typeof followUp === 'object') .map((followUp: any) => ({ description: followUp.description || 'No follow-up description', owner: followUp.owner || 'Unassigned', })), }, risks: { create: (analyzedData['Risks'] || []) .filter((risk: any) => risk && typeof risk === 'object') .map((risk: any) => ({ risk: risk.risk || 'No risk description', impact: risk.impact || 'No impact specified', })), }, agenda: { create: (analyzedData['Agenda'] || []) .filter((item: any) => item && typeof item === 'string') .map((item: string) => ({ item, })), }, }, include: { tasks: true, decisions: true, questions: true, insights: true, deadlines: true, attendees: true, followUps: true, risks: true, agenda: true, }, }); console.log('Meeting created:', { id: meeting.id, hasWordTimings: !!meeting.wordTimings, wordTimingsLength: meeting.wordTimings?.length }); // Send the response with segments and word timings return NextResponse.json( { ...meeting, segments: parsedTranscription.segments, wordTimings: parsedTranscription.word_timestamps, speakerLabels: meeting.speakerLabels ? JSON.parse(meeting.speakerLabels) : null, }, { status: 200 } ); } catch (error: any) { console.error('❌ Transcription error:', error); // Cleanup file if it exists and there was an error if (filePath && fs.existsSync(filePath)) { try { fs.unlinkSync(filePath); console.log('🗑️ Cleaned up file:', filePath); } catch (cleanupError) { console.error('Failed to cleanup file:', cleanupError); } } return NextResponse.json( { error: 'An error occurred during processing.', details: error.message }, { status: 500 } ); } };
```

# app\api\upload\route.ts

```ts
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'; import { DoclingProcessor, ProcessResult } from '@/lib/docling-processor'; import { prisma } from '@/lib/prisma'; import axios from 'axios'; import path from 'path'; import { writeFile, mkdir } from 'fs/promises'; import fs from 'fs'; const UPLOADS_DIR = path.join(process.cwd(), 'public', 'uploads'); interface ProcessedDocOutput { text: string; metadata: { title: string; author: string; subject: string; keywords: string; pageCount: number; } } export async function POST(request: NextRequest) { try { const formData = await request.formData(); const file = formData.get('file') as File; if (!file) { return NextResponse.json( { success: false, error: 'No file provided' }, { status: 400 } ); } // Create uploads directory if it doesn't exist try { await mkdir(UPLOADS_DIR, { recursive: true }); } catch (error) { console.error('Error creating upload directory:', error); } // Create a safe filename with timestamp const timestamp = Date.now(); const safeFilename = `${timestamp}-${file.name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9.-]/g, '_')}`; const filePath = path.join(UPLOADS_DIR, safeFilename); // Convert File to Buffer and save const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer(); const buffer = Buffer.from(arrayBuffer); await writeFile(filePath, buffer); let meetingData; // Process based on file type if (file.type === 'application/pdf') { // Process PDF using DoclingProcessor const result: ProcessResult = await DoclingProcessor.processDocument(filePath); if (!result.success) { console.error('Processing error:', result.error); return NextResponse.json( { success: false, error: result.error }, { status: 500 } ); } const parsedOutput = JSON.parse(result.output) as ProcessedDocOutput; meetingData = { name: parsedOutput.metadata.title || file.name, description: parsedOutput.metadata.subject || 'PDF Document', content: parsedOutput.text, documentFile: `/uploads/${safeFilename}`, metadata: { ...parsedOutput.metadata, fileName: file.name, fileSize: file.size, format: 'pdf', processedAt: new Date().toISOString() } }; } else if (file.type.startsWith('audio/')) { // Process audio using Langflow const payload = { output_type: "text", input_type: "text", tweaks: { "GroqWhisperComponent-d0YXz": { audio_file: filePath } } }; const response = await axios.post( process.env.LANGFLOW_TRANSCRIPTION_URL!, payload, { headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, params: { stream: false } } ); meetingData = { name: file.name, description: 'Audio Transcription', content: response.data.result, audioFile: `/uploads/${safeFilename}`, metadata: { fileName: file.name, fileSize: file.size, format: file.type, processedAt: new Date().toISOString() } }; } else { // Cleanup file if (fs.existsSync(filePath)) { fs.unlinkSync(filePath); } return NextResponse.json( { success: false, error: 'Unsupported file type' }, { status: 400 } ); } // Store in database const meeting = await prisma.meeting.create({ data: { name: meetingData.name, description: meetingData.description, rawTranscript: meetingData.content, summary: meetingData.content.slice(0, 200) + '...', // Create a brief summary audioFile: meetingData.audioFile, format: meetingData.metadata.format, fileSize: meetingData.metadata.fileSize, language: 'en', // Default to English, wordTimings: null, // Only applicable for audio files with diarization speakerLabels: null, // Only applicable for audio files with diarization confidence: null, // Only applicable for audio files duration: null // Only applicable for audio files } }); // Cleanup audio file after processing if it's an audio file if (file.type.startsWith('audio/') && fs.existsSync(filePath)) { fs.unlinkSync(filePath); } return NextResponse.json({ success: true, meeting }); } catch (error: any) { console.error('Request handling error:', error); return NextResponse.json( { success: false, error: error.message || 'Failed to handle request' }, { status: 500 } ); } }
```

# app\auth\signin\page.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import { signIn } from 'next-auth/react'; import { useSearchParams } from 'next/navigation'; import { Suspense } from 'react'; function SignInContent() { const searchParams = useSearchParams(); const error = searchParams.get('error'); const handleSignIn = () => { signIn('google', { callbackUrl: '/dashboard' }); }; return ( <> {error && ( <div className="mb-4 p-4 bg-red-50 text-red-600 rounded-md"> <p>Authentication error. Please try again.</p> </div> )} <button onClick={handleSignIn} className="flex items-center justify-center gap-2 px-6 py-3 bg-white text-gray-800 rounded-md border hover:bg-gray-50 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:ring-offset-2 transition-colors" > <svg className="w-5 h-5" viewBox="0 0 24 24"> <path fill="currentColor" d="M22.56 12.25c0-.78-.07-1.53-.2-2.25H12v4.26h5.92c-.26 1.37-1.04 2.53-2.21 3.31v2.77h3.57c2.08-1.92 3.28-4.74 3.28-8.09z" /> <path fill="currentColor" d="M12 23c2.97 0 5.46-.98 7.28-2.66l-3.57-2.77c-.98.66-2.23 1.06-3.71 1.06-2.86 0-5.29-1.93-6.16-4.53H2.18v2.84C3.99 20.53 7.7 23 12 23z" /> <path fill="currentColor" d="M5.84 14.09c-.22-.66-.35-1.36-.35-2.09s.13-1.43.35-2.09V7.07H2.18C1.43 8.55 1 10.22 1 12s.43 3.45 1.18 4.93l2.85-2.22.81-.62z" /> <path fill="currentColor" d="M12 5.38c1.62 0 3.06.56 4.21 1.64l3.15-3.15C17.45 2.09 14.97 1 12 1 7.7 1 3.99 3.47 2.18 7.07l3.66 2.84c.87-2.6 3.3-4.53 6.16-4.53z" /> </svg> Sign in with Google </button> </> ); } export default function SignIn() { return ( <div className="text-center"> <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6">Welcome to MeetingMind</h1> <Suspense fallback={<div>Loading...</div>}> <SignInContent /> </Suspense> </div> ); }
```

# app\dashboard\meeting\[id]\page.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import React, { useEffect, useState } from "react"; import { useParams } from "next/navigation"; import axios from "axios"; import MeetingDetails from "@/components/MeetingDetails"; import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation'; import { ArrowLeft } from 'lucide-react'; import type { MeetingWithParsedFields } from "@/types/global"; export default function MeetingPage() { const params = useParams(); const router = useRouter(); const meetingId = params.id as string; const [data, setData] = useState<MeetingWithParsedFields | null>(null); const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null); useEffect(() => { console.log("Fetching meeting details for ID:", meetingId); if (meetingId) { axios .get(`/api/meetings/${meetingId}`) .then((response) => { console.log("Received meeting data:", response.data); setData(response.data); }) .catch((error) => { console.error("Error fetching meeting details:", error); if (error.response && error.response.status === 404) { setError("Meeting not found."); } else { setError("Failed to fetch meeting details."); } }); } }, [meetingId]); const handleGoBack = () => { router.push('/dashboard'); }; if (error) { return ( <div className="container mx-auto p-6"> <button onClick={handleGoBack} className="mb-4 flex items-center text-purple-500 hover:text-purple-700"> <ArrowLeft className="mr-2" size={20} /> Back to Dashboard </button> <div className="text-red-500">{error}</div> </div> ); } if (!data) { return ( <div className="container mx-auto p-6"> <button onClick={handleGoBack} className="mb-4 flex items-center text-purple-500 hover:text-purple-700"> <ArrowLeft className="mr-2" size={20} /> Back to Dashboard </button> Loading... </div> ); } console.log("Rendering MeetingDetails with data:", data); return ( <div className="container mx-auto p-6"> <button onClick={handleGoBack} className="mb-4 flex items-center text-purple-500 hover:text-purple-700"> <ArrowLeft className="mr-2" size={20} /> Back to Dashboard </button> <MeetingDetails data={data} /> </div> ); }
```

# app\dashboard\page.tsx

```tsx
// app/dashboard/page.tsx 'use client'; import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'; import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button"; import { useRouter } from "next/navigation"; import axios from "axios"; import { Card, CardHeader, CardTitle, CardContent } from "@/components/ui/card"; import { Table, TableBody, TableCell, TableHead, TableHeader, TableRow } from "@/components/ui/table"; import { Checkbox } from "@/components/ui/checkbox"; import { FileAudio, FileText } from 'lucide-react'; import UploadModal from '@/components/UploadModal'; interface Meeting { id: string; name: string; description: string; audioFile?: string | null; } const Dashboard = () => { const router = useRouter(); const [meetings, setMeetings] = useState<Meeting[]>([]); const [selectedItems, setSelectedItems] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set()); const fetchMeetings = async () => { try { const response = await axios.get("/api/meetings"); setMeetings(response.data); } catch (error) { console.error("Error fetching meetings:", error); setMeetings([]); } }; useEffect(() => { fetchMeetings(); }, []); const handleViewDetails = (meeting: Meeting) => { if (meeting.audioFile) { router.push(`/dashboard/meeting/${meeting.id}`); } else { router.push(`/dashboard/document/${meeting.id}`); } }; const handleDelete = async (meetingId: string) => { if (confirm("Are you sure you want to delete this item?")) { try { await axios.delete(`/api/meetings/${meetingId}`); fetchMeetings(); } catch (error) { console.error("Error deleting meeting:", error); } } }; const handleCheckboxChange = (id: string) => { const newSelected = new Set(selectedItems); if (newSelected.has(id)) { newSelected.delete(id); } else { newSelected.add(id); } setSelectedItems(newSelected); }; return ( <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-100 p-6"> <header className="mb-8"> <div className="flex justify-between items-center"> <div> <h1 className="text-4xl font-bold text-blue-600">Meeting Mind</h1> <p className="text-gray-500">Content Library</p> </div> <UploadModal onUploadSuccess={fetchMeetings} /> </div> </header> <Card> <CardHeader> <CardTitle>Previous Content</CardTitle> </CardHeader> <CardContent> {meetings.length > 0 ? ( <Table> <TableHeader> <TableRow> <TableHead className="w-12">Select</TableHead> <TableHead>Type</TableHead> <TableHead>Name</TableHead> <TableHead>Description</TableHead> <TableHead>Actions</TableHead> </TableRow> </TableHeader> <TableBody> {meetings.map((meeting) => ( <TableRow key={meeting.id}> <TableCell> <Checkbox checked={selectedItems.has(meeting.id)} onCheckedChange={() => handleCheckboxChange(meeting.id)} /> </TableCell> <TableCell> {meeting.audioFile ? ( <FileAudio className="h-5 w-5 text-blue-500" /> ) : ( <FileText className="h-5 w-5 text-green-500" /> )} </TableCell> <TableCell>{meeting.name}</TableCell> <TableCell>{meeting.description}</TableCell> <TableCell> <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => handleViewDetails(meeting)} className="mr-2" > View Details </Button> <Button variant="destructive" onClick={() => handleDelete(meeting.id)} > Delete </Button> </TableCell> </TableRow> ))} </TableBody> </Table> ) : ( <p className="text-gray-500">No content found.</p> )} </CardContent> </Card> </div> ); }; export default Dashboard;
```

# app\error\page.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import { useSearchParams } from 'next/navigation'; import Link from 'next/link'; import { Suspense } from 'react'; function ErrorContent() { const searchParams = useSearchParams(); const error = searchParams.get('error'); const getErrorMessage = (error: string | null) => { switch (error) { case 'Callback': return 'There was an error during the Google sign-in process. This might be due to:'; case 'AccessDenied': return 'Access was denied to your account.'; case 'Configuration': return 'There is a problem with the server configuration.'; default: return 'An unknown error occurred.'; } }; const getErrorDetails = (error: string | null) => { if (error === 'Callback') { return [ 'The Google sign-in process was interrupted', 'Your browser blocked third-party cookies', 'The OAuth configuration might need to be verified' ]; } return []; }; return ( <> <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-red-600">Authentication Error</h1> <div className="mt-4 text-gray-600"> <p className="mb-4">{getErrorMessage(error)}</p> {getErrorDetails(error).length > 0 && ( <ul className="list-disc text-left pl-6 mb-4 space-y-2"> {getErrorDetails(error).map((detail, index) => ( <li key={index}>{detail}</li> ))} </ul> )} </div> <div className="mt-6 space-y-4"> <Link href="/auth/signin" className="block w-full px-4 py-2 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-blue-700 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2 focus:ring-blue-500" > Try Again </Link> <Link href="/" className="block w-full px-4 py-2 bg-gray-200 text-gray-700 rounded-md hover:bg-gray-300 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2 focus:ring-gray-500" > Return Home </Link> </div> </> ); } export default function ErrorPage() { return ( <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-gray-50"> <div className="max-w-md w-full space-y-8 p-8 bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg text-center"> <Suspense fallback={<div>Loading...</div>}> <ErrorContent /> </Suspense> </div> </div> ); }
```

# app\providers.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import { SessionProvider } from 'next-auth/react'; import { ReactNode } from 'react'; import { ErrorBoundary } from 'react-error-boundary'; interface ProvidersProps { children: ReactNode; } function ErrorFallback({error}: {error: Error}) { return ( <div className="text-red-500"> Something went wrong: {error.message} </div> ); } export default function Providers({ children }: ProvidersProps) { return ( <ErrorBoundary FallbackComponent={ErrorFallback}> <SessionProvider>{children}</SessionProvider> </ErrorBoundary> ); }
```

# app\server\page.tsx

```tsx
'use client' import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation' import { useState } from 'react' export default function ServerUploadPage() { const router = useRouter() const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null) const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false) async function upload(data: FormData) { setLoading(true) setError(null) const file: File | null = data.get('file') as unknown as File if (!file) { setError('No file uploaded') setLoading(false) return } // Check if file is PDF if (file.type !== 'application/pdf') { setError('Please upload a PDF file') setLoading(false) return } try { // Store the file in sessionStorage to pass it to the test-document page const reader = new FileReader() reader.onload = () => { sessionStorage.setItem('uploadedFile', JSON.stringify({ name: file.name, type: file.type, data: reader.result })) // Redirect to test-document page router.push('/test-document') } reader.readAsDataURL(file) } catch (err) { console.error('Upload error:', err) setError('Failed to process file') } finally { setLoading(false) } } return ( <main className="p-8"> <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">Upload PDF Document</h1> <form action={upload}> <input type="file" name="file" accept=".pdf,application/pdf" className="mb-4 block" disabled={loading} /> {error && ( <p className="text-red-500 mb-4">{error}</p> )} <input type="submit" value={loading ? "Processing..." : "Upload"} disabled={loading} className="px-4 py-2 bg-blue-500 text-white rounded hover:bg-blue-600 cursor-pointer disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed" /> </form> </main> ) }
```

# app\test-analysis\page.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import React, { useState } from 'react'; import { Card, CardHeader, CardTitle, CardContent } from 'components/ui/card'; import { Button } from 'components/ui/button'; import { Textarea } from 'components/ui/text-area'; import { Label } from 'components/ui/label'; import { useToast } from 'hooks/use-toast'; import { AnalysisDisplay } from 'components/test/AnalysisDisplay'; interface AnalysisResult { Breakdown: { tasks: Array<{ description: string; assigned_to: string; priority: string; }>; decisions: Array<{ description: string; }>; questions: Array<{ question: string; raised_by: string; status: string; answer?: string; }>; insights: Array<{ description: string; }>; deadlines: Array<{ description: string; date: string; }>; attendees: Array<{ name: string; role: string; }>; follow_ups: Array<{ description: string; owner: string; due_date: string; }>; risks: Array<{ description: string; impact: string; }>; agenda: Array<string>; meeting_name: string; description: string; summary: string; }; } export default function TestAnalysis() { // State management const [transcriptText, setTranscriptText] = useState(''); const [isAnalyzing, setIsAnalyzing] = useState(false); const [analysisResult, setAnalysisResult] = useState<AnalysisResult | null>(null); const { toast } = useToast(); // Handlers const handleTextChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLTextAreaElement>) => { setTranscriptText(e.target.value); // Reset analysis when text changes if (analysisResult) { setAnalysisResult(null); } }; const handleAnalyze = async () => { if (!transcriptText.trim()) return; setIsAnalyzing(true); setAnalysisResult(null); try { const response = await fetch('/api/test-analyze', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', }, body: JSON.stringify({ transcriptionText: transcriptText, timestamp: Date.now().toString() }) }); if (!response.ok) { throw new Error(`Analysis failed with status: ${response.status}`); } const data = await response.json(); console.log('Analysis response:', data); // Extract the message containing the JSON string const message = data.outputs?.[0]?.outputs?.[0]?.messages?.[0]?.message; if (!message) { throw new Error('Invalid analysis response format'); } // Extract JSON from the markdown code block const jsonMatch = message.match(/\`\`\`json\s*([\s\S]*?)\s*\`\`\`/); if (!jsonMatch) { throw new Error('Could not find JSON data in response'); } // Parse the extracted JSON const parsedAnalysis = JSON.parse(jsonMatch[1].trim()); // Map the data to match the expected interface setAnalysisResult({ Breakdown: { tasks: parsedAnalysis.Tasks.map(task => ({ description: task.task, assigned_to: task.owner, priority: task.priority })), decisions: parsedAnalysis.Decisions.map(decision => ({ description: decision.decision })), questions: parsedAnalysis.Questions.map(question => ({ question: question.question, raised_by: '', status: question.status, answer: question.answer })), insights: parsedAnalysis.Insights.map(insight => ({ description: insight.insight })), deadlines: parsedAnalysis.Deadlines.map(deadline => ({ description: deadline.deadline, date: deadline.date })), attendees: parsedAnalysis.Attendees.map(attendee => ({ name: attendee.name, role: attendee.role })), follow_ups: parsedAnalysis["Follow-ups"].map(followUp => ({ description: followUp.follow_up, owner: followUp.owner, due_date: followUp.due_date })), risks: parsedAnalysis.Risks.map(risk => ({ description: risk.risk, impact: risk.impact })), agenda: parsedAnalysis.Agenda, meeting_name: parsedAnalysis["Meeting Name"], description: parsedAnalysis.Description, summary: parsedAnalysis.Summary } }); toast({ title: 'Analysis Complete', description: 'Transcript has been analyzed successfully.', }); } catch (error) { console.error('Analysis error:', error); toast({ title: 'Analysis Failed', description: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to analyze transcript', variant: 'destructive', }); } finally { setIsAnalyzing(false); } }; return ( <div className="container mx-auto p-6"> <div className="space-y-6"> <Card> <CardHeader> <CardTitle>Analysis Test</CardTitle> </CardHeader> <CardContent className="space-y-4"> <div className="space-y-2"> <Label htmlFor="transcript">Transcript Text</Label> <Textarea id="transcript" placeholder="Paste transcript text here..." value={transcriptText} onChange={handleTextChange} rows={10} className="font-mono min-h-[200px] w-full" disabled={isAnalyzing} /> </div> <Button onClick={handleAnalyze} disabled={isAnalyzing || !transcriptText.trim()} className="w-full" > {isAnalyzing ? ( <span className="animate-pulse">Analyzing...</span> ) : ( 'Analyze Transcript' )} </Button> </CardContent> </Card> {analysisResult && ( <AnalysisDisplay analysis={analysisResult.Breakdown} /> )} </div> </div> ); }
```

# app\test-docling\page.tsx

```tsx
// app/test-docling/page.tsx 'use client'; import React, { useState } from 'react'; import { Card, CardHeader, CardTitle, CardContent } from "@/components/ui/card"; import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button"; import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input"; import { DocumentViewer } from "@/components/test/DocumentViewer"; import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast"; import { Upload, FileType, LoaderCircle } from 'lucide-react'; interface ProcessingResult { success: boolean; output: string; processedFile?: string; } export default function TestDoclingPage() { const [file, setFile] = useState<File | null>(null); const [isProcessing, setIsProcessing] = useState(false); const [result, setResult] = useState<ProcessingResult | null>(null); const { toast } = useToast(); const handleFileChange = (event: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => { const selectedFile = event.target.files?.[0]; if (selectedFile) { setFile(selectedFile); setResult(null); } }; const handleProcess = async () => { if (!file) { toast({ title: "Error", description: "Please select a file first", variant: "destructive", }); return; } setIsProcessing(true); const formData = new FormData(); formData.append('file', file); formData.append('type', 'process'); try { const response = await fetch('/api/test-docling', { method: 'POST', body: formData, }); const data = await response.json(); if (!response.ok) { throw new Error(data.error || 'Processing failed'); } setResult(data); toast({ title: "Success", description: "Document processed successfully", }); } catch (error) { console.error('Processing error:', error); toast({ title: "Error", description: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to process document', variant: "destructive", }); } finally { setIsProcessing(false); } }; return ( <div className="container mx-auto p-6"> <Card> <CardHeader> <CardTitle>Test Docling</CardTitle> </CardHeader> <CardContent className="space-y-4"> <div className="flex flex-col gap-4"> <div className="grid w-full max-w-sm items-center gap-1.5"> <Input type="file" onChange={handleFileChange} accept=".txt,.doc,.docx,.pdf" disabled={isProcessing} className="cursor-pointer" /> </div> <Button onClick={handleProcess} disabled={!file || isProcessing} className="w-full max-w-sm" > {isProcessing ? ( <> <LoaderCircle className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin" /> Processing... </> ) : ( <> <Upload className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> Process Document </> )} </Button> </div> {result && ( <div className="mt-6"> <DocumentViewer content={result.output} title="Processing Result" maxHeight="400px" /> </div> )} </CardContent> </Card> </div> ); }
```

# app\test-document\page.tsx

```tsx
'use client' import { useState } from 'react' import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '../../components/ui/card' import { ScrollArea } from '../../components/ui/scroll-area' import { Button } from '../../components/ui/button' import { Upload } from 'lucide-react' import { useToast } from '../../hooks/use-toast' export default function TestDocument() { const [content, setContent] = useState<{text: string; metadata: any} | null>(null); const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false); const { toast } = useToast(); async function handleFileUpload(e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) { const file = e.target.files?.[0]; if (!file) return; // Check if file is PDF if (file.type !== 'application/pdf') { toast({ title: "Invalid file type", description: "Please upload a PDF file", variant: "destructive" }); return; } setLoading(true); try { const formData = new FormData(); formData.append('file', file); const response = await fetch('/api/test-document', { method: 'POST', body: formData, }); if (!response.ok) { const error = await response.json(); throw new Error(error.error || 'Failed to process document'); } const result = await response.json(); setContent(result); toast({ title: "Document processed", description: `Successfully processed ${file.name}`, }); } catch (error) { console.error('Upload error:', error); toast({ title: "Processing failed", description: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to process document', variant: "destructive" }); } finally { setLoading(false); } } return ( <div className="container mx-auto py-8"> <Card className="w-full"> <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between"> <CardTitle>Document Viewer (Test)</CardTitle> <div className="flex items-center gap-4"> <Button variant="outline" size="icon" asChild> <label className="cursor-pointer"> <Upload className="h-4 w-4" /> <input type="file" className="hidden" accept=".pdf" onChange={handleFileUpload} disabled={loading} /> </label> </Button> </div> </CardHeader> <CardContent> <ScrollArea className="h-[600px] w-full rounded-md border"> <div className="p-4"> {loading ? ( <div className="flex justify-center p-4"> <div className="text-muted-foreground">Processing document...</div> </div> ) : content ? ( <div className="space-y-4"> <div className="prose"> <h3>Extracted Text</h3> <pre className="whitespace-pre-wrap font-mono text-sm bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded"> {content.text} </pre> </div> {content.metadata && Object.keys(content.metadata).length > 0 && ( <div className="prose"> <h3>Metadata</h3> <pre className="whitespace-pre-wrap font-mono text-sm bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded"> {JSON.stringify(content.metadata, null, 2)} </pre> </div> )} </div> ) : ( <div className="text-center text-muted-foreground"> Upload a PDF document to view its contents </div> )} </div> </ScrollArea> </CardContent> </Card> </div> ); }
```

# app\test-mock\page.tsx

```tsx
// app/test-mock/page.tsx 'use client'; import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button"; import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast"; import { useState } from "react"; export default function TestMock() { const { toast } = useToast(); const [result, setResult] = useState<any>(null); const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false); const handleTest = async () => { setIsLoading(true); try { const response = await fetch('/api/test-data', { method: 'POST' }); const data = await response.json(); setResult(data); toast({ title: "Success", description: "Mock data loaded successfully", }); } catch (error) { console.error(error); toast({ title: "Error", description: "Failed to load mock data", variant: "destructive", }); } finally { setIsLoading(false); } }; return ( <div className="p-8"> <Button onClick={handleTest} disabled={isLoading}> {isLoading ? 'Loading...' : 'Test Mock Data'} </Button> {result && ( <pre className="mt-4 p-4 bg-gray-100 rounded overflow-auto"> {JSON.stringify(result, null, 2)} </pre> )} </div> ); }
```

# app\test-transcribe\page.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import React, { useState } from 'react'; import { Card, CardHeader, CardTitle, CardContent } from 'components/ui/card'; import { Button } from 'components/ui/button'; import { Input } from 'components/ui/input'; import { Label } from 'components/ui/label'; import { FFmpeg } from '@ffmpeg/ffmpeg'; import { fetchFile } from '@ffmpeg/util'; import { useToast } from 'hooks/use-toast'; import { TranscriptionPlayer } from 'components/test/TranscriptionPlayer'; import { AnalysisDisplay } from 'components/test/AnalysisDisplay'; import type { TranscriptSegment } from 'types/global'; // Initialize ffmpeg lazily let ffmpeg: FFmpeg | null = null; interface TranscriptionResult { text: string; segments: TranscriptSegment[] | null; word_timestamps?: any[]; } interface AnalysisResult { Breakdown: { tasks: Array<{ description: string; assigned_to: string; priority: string; }>; decisions: Array<{ description: string; }>; questions: Array<{ question: string; raised_by: string; status: string; answer?: string; }>; insights: Array<{ description: string; }>; deadlines: Array<{ description: string; date: string; }>; attendees: Array<{ name: string; role: string; }>; follow_ups: Array<{ description: string; owner: string; due_date: string; }>; risks: Array<{ description: string; impact: string; }>; agenda: Array<string>; meeting_name: string; description: string; summary: string; }; } export default function TestTranscribe() { const [file, setFile] = useState<File | null>(null); const [isCompressing, setIsCompressing] = useState(false); const [isTranscribing, setIsTranscribing] = useState(false); const [isAnalyzing, setIsAnalyzing] = useState(false); const [transcriptionResult, setTranscriptionResult] = useState<TranscriptionResult | null>(null); const [analysisResult, setAnalysisResult] = useState<AnalysisResult | null>(null); const [audioUrl, setAudioUrl] = useState<string>(''); const { toast } = useToast(); const loadFFmpeg = async () => { if (!ffmpeg) { ffmpeg = new FFmpeg(); } if (!ffmpeg.loaded) { await ffmpeg.load(); } }; const handleFileChange = (event: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => { const selectedFile = event.target.files?.[0]; if (selectedFile) { if (audioUrl) { URL.revokeObjectURL(audioUrl); } setFile(selectedFile); setAudioUrl(URL.createObjectURL(selectedFile)); setTranscriptionResult(null); setAnalysisResult(null); } }; const handleCompress = async () => { if (!file) return; setIsCompressing(true); try { await loadFFmpeg(); if (!ffmpeg) throw new Error('FFmpeg not initialized'); await ffmpeg.writeFile('input_audio', await fetchFile(file)); await ffmpeg.exec([ '-i', 'input_audio', '-ar', '16000', '-ac', '1', '-b:a', '64k', 'output_audio.mp3' ]); const data = await ffmpeg.readFile('output_audio.mp3'); const compressedBlob = new Blob([data], { type: 'audio/mpeg' }); const compressedFile = new File([compressedBlob], `compressed_${file.name}`, { type: 'audio/mpeg', }); if (audioUrl) { URL.revokeObjectURL(audioUrl); } setFile(compressedFile); setAudioUrl(URL.createObjectURL(compressedFile)); toast({ title: 'Compression Complete', description: `File size reduced to ${(compressedFile.size / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(2)} MB`, }); } catch (error) { console.error('Compression error:', error); toast({ title: 'Compression Failed', description: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to compress audio', variant: 'destructive', }); } finally { setIsCompressing(false); } }; const handleTranscribe = async () => { if (!file) return; setIsTranscribing(true); setTranscriptionResult(null); setAnalysisResult(null); const formData = new FormData(); formData.append('audio', file); formData.append('type', 'transcription'); formData.append('timestamp', Date.now().toString()); try { const response = await fetch('/api/test-transcribe', { method: 'POST', body: formData, }); if (!response.ok) { const errorData = await response.json(); throw new Error(errorData.error || `Transcription failed with status: ${response.status}`); } const data = await response.json(); console.log('Raw API response:', data); // Extract text from the correct path in the response const transcriptionMessage = data.outputs?.[0]?.outputs?.[0]?.messages?.[0]?.message; if (!transcriptionMessage) { throw new Error('Invalid transcription response format'); } // Parse the JSON string in the message const parsedTranscription = JSON.parse(transcriptionMessage); setTranscriptionResult({ text: parsedTranscription.text || '', segments: parsedTranscription.segments || null, word_timestamps: parsedTranscription.word_timestamps || [] }); toast({ title: 'Transcription Complete', description: 'Audio has been transcribed successfully.', }); } catch (error) { console.error('Transcription error:', error); toast({ title: 'Transcription Failed', description: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to transcribe audio', variant: 'destructive', }); } finally { setIsTranscribing(false); } }; const handleAnalyze = async () => { if (!transcriptionResult?.text) return; setIsAnalyzing(true); setAnalysisResult(null); const formData = new FormData(); formData.append('type', 'analysis'); formData.append('transcriptionText', transcriptionResult.text); formData.append('timestamp', Date.now().toString()); try { const response = await fetch('/api/test-analyze', { method: 'POST', body: formData, }); if (!response.ok) { throw new Error(`Analysis failed with status: ${response.status}`); } const data = await response.json(); setAnalysisResult(data as AnalysisResult); toast({ title: 'Analysis Complete', description: 'Transcript has been analyzed successfully.', }); } catch (error) { console.error('Analysis error:', error); toast({ title: 'Analysis Failed', description: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to analyze transcript', variant: 'destructive', }); } finally { setIsAnalyzing(false); } }; React.useEffect(() => { return () => { if (audioUrl) { URL.revokeObjectURL(audioUrl); } }; }, []); return ( <div className="container mx-auto p-6"> <div className="space-y-6"> <Card> <CardHeader> <CardTitle>Audio File Selection</CardTitle> </CardHeader> <CardContent className="space-y-4"> <div> <Label htmlFor="audio-file">Select Audio File</Label> <Input id="audio-file" type="file" accept="audio/*" onChange={handleFileChange} disabled={isTranscribing || isAnalyzing} /> </div> {file && ( <div> <p>File size: {(file.size / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(2)} MB</p> {file.size > 25 * 1024 * 1024 && ( <Button onClick={handleCompress} disabled={isCompressing}> {isCompressing ? 'Compressing...' : 'Compress Audio'} </Button> )} </div> )} </CardContent> </Card> <Card> <CardHeader> <CardTitle>Processing Controls</CardTitle> </CardHeader> <CardContent className="space-x-4"> <Button onClick={handleTranscribe} disabled={!file || isTranscribing || file.size > 25 * 1024 * 1024} > {isTranscribing ? 'Transcribing...' : 'Transcribe'} </Button> <Button onClick={handleAnalyze} disabled={!transcriptionResult || isAnalyzing} > {isAnalyzing ? 'Analyzing...' : 'Analyze'} </Button> </CardContent> </Card> {transcriptionResult && ( <TranscriptionPlayer audioUrl={audioUrl} transcript={transcriptionResult.text} segments={transcriptionResult.segments} /> )} {analysisResult && ( <AnalysisDisplay analysis={analysisResult.Breakdown} /> )} </div> </div> ); }
```

# app\testapi\page.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import { useState } from 'react'; import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button'; import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input'; import { Card } from '@/components/ui/card'; import { useToast } from '@/hooks/use-toast'; export default function TestAPI() { const [file, setFile] = useState<File | null>(null); const [result, setResult] = useState<string>(''); const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false); const { toast } = useToast(); const handleFileChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => { if (e.target.files && e.target.files[0]) { setFile(e.target.files[0]); } }; const handleSubmit = async () => { if (!file) { toast({ title: 'Erro', description: 'Por favor selecione um arquivo', variant: 'destructive', }); return; } setLoading(true); try { const formData = new FormData(); formData.append('file', file); const response = await fetch('http://localhost:8000/api/v1/documents/process', { method: 'POST', body: formData, }); if (!response.ok) { throw new Error('Erro ao processar arquivo'); } const data = await response.json(); setResult(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)); toast({ title: 'Sucesso', description: 'Arquivo processado com sucesso', }); } catch (error) { console.error('Erro:', error); toast({ title: 'Erro', description: 'Falha ao processar arquivo', variant: 'destructive', }); } finally { setLoading(false); } }; return ( <div className="container mx-auto p-8"> <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6">Teste Docling API</h1> <Card className="p-6 mb-6"> <div className="space-y-4"> <div> <Input type="file" onChange={handleFileChange} accept=".pdf,.doc,.docx,.pptx,.html,.jpg,.jpeg,.png" className="mb-4" /> </div> <Button onClick={handleSubmit} disabled={loading} > {loading ? 'Processando...' : 'Processar Arquivo'} </Button> </div> </Card> {result && ( <Card className="p-6"> <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-4">Resultado:</h2> <pre className="bg-gray-100 p-4 rounded-lg overflow-auto max-h-[500px]"> {result} </pre> </Card> )} </div> ); }
```
