# components\AudioPlayer.tsx

```tsx
"use client" import React, { useRef, useState, useEffect } from 'react' interface AudioPlayerProps { audioUrl: string } export default function AudioPlayer({ audioUrl }: AudioPlayerProps) { const audioRef = useRef<HTMLAudioElement>(null) const [isPlaying, setIsPlaying] = useState(false) const [currentTime, setCurrentTime] = useState(0) const [duration, setDuration] = useState(0) useEffect(() => { const audio = audioRef.current if (!audio) return const handleLoadedMetadata = () => { setDuration(audio.duration) } const handleTimeUpdate = () => { setCurrentTime(audio.currentTime) } const handleEnded = () => { setIsPlaying(false) setCurrentTime(0) } audio.addEventListener('loadedmetadata', handleLoadedMetadata) audio.addEventListener('timeupdate', handleTimeUpdate) audio.addEventListener('ended', handleEnded) return () => { audio.removeEventListener('loadedmetadata', handleLoadedMetadata) audio.removeEventListener('timeupdate', handleTimeUpdate) audio.removeEventListener('ended', handleEnded) } }, []) const togglePlayPause = () => { if (audioRef.current) { if (isPlaying) { audioRef.current.pause() } else { audioRef.current.play() } setIsPlaying(!isPlaying) } } const handleSeek = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => { const time = parseFloat(e.target.value) if (audioRef.current) { audioRef.current.currentTime = time setCurrentTime(time) } } const formatTime = (time: number) => { const minutes = Math.floor(time / 60) const seconds = Math.floor(time % 60) return `${minutes}:${seconds.toString().padStart(2, '0')}` } return ( <div className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 bg-background border-t border-border p-4 shadow-lg"> <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto flex items-center gap-4"> <button onClick={togglePlayPause} className="w-10 h-10 flex items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90" > {isPlaying ? ( <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"> <rect x="6" y="4" width="4" height="16"></rect> <rect x="14" y="4" width="4" height="16"></rect> </svg> ) : ( <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"> <polygon points="5 3 19 12 5 21 5 3"></polygon> </svg> )} </button> <span className="text-sm">{formatTime(currentTime)}</span> <input type="range" min="0" max={duration || 0} value={currentTime} onChange={handleSeek} className="flex-1 h-2 bg-secondary rounded-lg appearance-none cursor-pointer" /> <span className="text-sm">{formatTime(duration)}</span> <audio ref={audioRef} src={audioUrl} /> </div> </div> ) }
```

# components\AudioTranscriptPlayer.tsx

```tsx
// AudioTranscriptPlayer.tsx import React, { useRef, useState, useEffect } from 'react'; import { Card, CardContent } from 'components/ui/card'; import type { TranscriptSegment } from 'types/global'; interface AudioTranscriptPlayerProps { audioUrl?: string; transcript?: string; segments: TranscriptSegment[] | null; } const AudioTranscriptPlayer: React.FC<AudioTranscriptPlayerProps> = ({ audioUrl = '', transcript = '', segments = null }) => { const audioRef = useRef<HTMLAudioElement | null>(null); const [currentTime, setCurrentTime] = useState(0); const [isPlaying, setIsPlaying] = useState(false); const [duration, setDuration] = useState(0); const [currentSegmentIndex, setCurrentSegmentIndex] = useState(-1); const timeUpdateRef = useRef<number>(0); // Parse segments and add debug log const parsedSegments = React.useMemo(() => { console.log('AudioTranscriptPlayer received:', { hasSegments: !!segments, segmentsType: typeof segments, segmentsLength: segments?.length, firstFewSegments: segments?.slice(0, 5), audioUrl, transcriptLength: transcript?.length }); if (!segments || !Array.isArray(segments)) { console.log('No segments available or invalid format'); return []; } // Ensure segments are properly structured const validSegments = segments.filter(segment => { const isValid = segment && typeof segment === 'object' && typeof segment.text === 'string' && typeof segment.start === 'number' && typeof segment.end === 'number'; if (!isValid) { console.error('Invalid segment object:', segment); } return isValid; }); console.log('Filtered segments:', { original: segments.length, filtered: validSegments.length, sample: validSegments.slice(0, 5) }); return validSegments; }, [segments, transcript, audioUrl]); // Function to find current segment index const findCurrentSegmentIndex = (currentTime: number) => { if (parsedSegments.length === 0) return -1; // Find the segment that matches the current time const index = parsedSegments.findIndex( segment => currentTime >= segment.start && currentTime <= segment.end ); // If no exact match, find the closest upcoming segment if (index === -1) { const nextSegmentIndex = parsedSegments.findIndex( segment => currentTime < segment.start ); return nextSegmentIndex > 0 ? nextSegmentIndex - 1 : -1; } return index; }; useEffect(() => { const audio = audioRef.current; if (!audio) return; const handleLoadedMetadata = () => { console.log('Audio metadata loaded:', { duration: audio.duration, src: audio.src }); setDuration(audio.duration); }; const handleTimeUpdate = () => { const now = Date.now(); // Throttle updates to every 100ms if (now - timeUpdateRef.current < 100) return; timeUpdateRef.current = now; const currentTime = audio.currentTime; setCurrentTime(currentTime); // Find the current segment based on timestamp const index = findCurrentSegmentIndex(currentTime); if (index !== currentSegmentIndex) { setCurrentSegmentIndex(index); console.log('Current segment update:', { time: currentTime, index, text: parsedSegments[index]?.text, timing: parsedSegments[index], totalSegments: parsedSegments.length }); } }; const handleEnded = () => { setIsPlaying(false); setCurrentTime(0); setCurrentSegmentIndex(-1); }; const handlePlay = () => { console.log('Audio started playing'); setIsPlaying(true); }; const handlePause = () => { console.log('Audio paused'); setIsPlaying(false); }; audio.addEventListener('loadedmetadata', handleLoadedMetadata); audio.addEventListener('timeupdate', handleTimeUpdate); audio.addEventListener('ended', handleEnded); audio.addEventListener('play', handlePlay); audio.addEventListener('pause', handlePause); return () => { audio.removeEventListener('loadedmetadata', handleLoadedMetadata); audio.removeEventListener('timeupdate', handleTimeUpdate); audio.removeEventListener('ended', handleEnded); audio.removeEventListener('play', handlePlay); audio.removeEventListener('pause', handlePause); }; }, [parsedSegments, currentSegmentIndex]); const handleSegmentClick = (index: number) => { if (audioRef.current && parsedSegments[index]) { const time = parsedSegments[index].start; console.log('Seeking to segment:', { index, text: parsedSegments[index].text, time }); audioRef.current.currentTime = time; if (!isPlaying) { audioRef.current.play(); } } }; const togglePlayPause = () => { if (audioRef.current) { if (isPlaying) { audioRef.current.pause(); } else { audioRef.current.play(); } } }; const handleSeek = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => { const time = parseFloat(e.target.value); if (audioRef.current) { console.log('Manual seek to:', time); audioRef.current.currentTime = time; setCurrentTime(time); } }; const formatTime = (time: number) => { const minutes = Math.floor(time / 60); const seconds = Math.floor(time % 60); return `${minutes}:${seconds.toString().padStart(2, '0')}`; }; if (!audioUrl) { return ( <Card className="w-full"> <CardContent className="p-6"> <p className="text-muted-foreground">No audio file available</p> </CardContent> </Card> ); } return ( <Card className="w-full"> <CardContent className="p-6"> <div className="space-y-4"> {/* Transcript display */} <div className="max-h-48 overflow-y-auto p-4 bg-muted rounded-lg text-base leading-relaxed"> {parsedSegments.length > 0 ? ( <div className="inline"> {parsedSegments.map((segment, index) => ( <span key={`${index}-${segment.start}`} onClick={() => handleSegmentClick(index)} className={`cursor-pointer inline transition-colors duration-200 px-1 rounded ${index === currentSegmentIndex ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground' : 'hover:text-primary' }`} > {segment.text} </span> ))} </div> ) : ( <p className="text-muted-foreground">No transcript available</p> )} </div> {/* Audio controls */} <div className="flex items-center gap-4"> <button onClick={togglePlayPause} className="w-10 h-10 flex items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90" aria-label={isPlaying ? 'Pause' : 'Play'} > {isPlaying ? ( <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" className="w-6 h-6"> <rect x="6" y="4" width="4" height="16" /> <rect x="14" y="4" width="4" height="16" /> </svg> ) : ( <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" className="w-6 h-6"> <polygon points="5 3 19 12 5 21 5 3" /> </svg> )} </button> <span className="text-sm tabular-nums"> {formatTime(currentTime)} </span> <input type="range" min="0" max={duration || 0} value={currentTime} onChange={handleSeek} className="flex-1 h-2 bg-secondary rounded-lg appearance-none cursor-pointer" aria-label="Audio progress" /> <span className="text-sm tabular-nums"> {formatTime(duration)} </span> </div> </div> <audio ref={audioRef} src={audioUrl} preload="metadata" /> </CardContent> </Card> ); }; export default AudioTranscriptPlayer;
```

```tsx
'use client'; import { signIn, signOut, useSession } from 'next-auth/react'; import { Button } from './ui/button'; import { useState } from 'react'; export default function AuthPopupButton() { const { data: session, status } = useSession(); const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false); const handleAuth = async () => { try { setIsLoading(true); if (session) { await signOut({ callbackUrl: '/' }); } else { // Direct sign in without going through the signin page await signIn('google', { callbackUrl: '/dashboard', redirect: true, }); } } catch (error) { console.error('Auth error:', error); } finally { setIsLoading(false); } }; return ( <Button onClick={handleAuth} disabled={status === 'loading' || isLoading} className="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2" > {status === 'loading' ? ( 'Loading...' ) : session ? ( 'Sign Out' ) : ( <> <svg className="h-5 w-5" viewBox="0 0 24 24"> <path fill="currentColor" d="M22.56 12.25c0-.78-.07-1.53-.2-2.25H12v4.26h5.92c-.26 1.37-1.04 2.53-2.21 3.31v2.77h3.57c2.08-1.92 3.28-4.74 3.28-8.09z" /> <path fill="currentColor" d="M12 23c2.97 0 5.46-.98 7.28-2.66l-3.57-2.77c-.98.66-2.23 1.06-3.71 1.06-2.86 0-5.29-1.93-6.16-4.53H2.18v2.84C3.99 20.53 7.7 23 12 23z" /> <path fill="currentColor" d="M5.84 14.09c-.22-.66-.35-1.36-.35-2.09s.13-1.43.35-2.09V7.07H2.18C1.43 8.55 1 10.22 1 12s.43 3.45 1.18 4.93l2.85-2.22.81-.62z" /> <path fill="currentColor" d="M12 5.38c1.62 0 3.06.56 4.21 1.64l3.15-3.15C17.45 2.09 14.97 1 12 1 7.7 1 3.99 3.47 2.18 7.07l3.66 2.84c.87-2.6 3.3-4.53 6.16-4.53z" /> </svg> Continue with Google </> )} </Button> ); }
```

# components\CategoryCard.tsx

```tsx
"use client" import React from "react" import { ScrollArea } from "@/components/ui/scroll-area" import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card" interface CategoryItem { [key: string]: string | Date | null; } interface CategoryProps { title: string; items: CategoryItem[]; gridSpan?: string; } const CategoryCard: React.FC<CategoryProps> = ({ title, items, gridSpan }) => { const formatValue = (value: string | Date | null): string => { if (value === null) return 'N/A'; if (value instanceof Date) return value.toISOString().split('T')[0]; if (typeof value === 'string' && value.includes('T')) { return value.split('T')[0]; } return value; }; return ( <Card className={`h-full ${gridSpan}`}> <CardHeader> <CardTitle>{title}</CardTitle> </CardHeader> <CardContent> <ScrollArea className="h-[200px] pr-4"> {items.length === 0 ? ( <p className="text-muted-foreground">No items available.</p> ) : ( <ul className="space-y-2"> {items.map((item, index) => ( <li key={index} className="bg-muted p-2 rounded-md"> {Object.entries(item).map(([key, value]) => { const formattedKey = key .split('_') .map(word => word.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + word.slice(1)) .join(' '); const formattedValue = formatValue(value); return ( <div key={key}> <strong className="text-primary">{formattedKey}:</strong>{' '} {formattedValue} </div> ); })} </li> ))} </ul> )} </ScrollArea> </CardContent> </Card> ); }; export default CategoryCard;
```

# components\DocumentDisplay.tsx

```tsx
import { ScrollArea } from './ui/scroll-area'; import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from './ui/card'; import { documentStyles, documentContainerStyles, metadataStyles } from './ui/document-styles'; import { Badge } from 'components/ui/badge'; import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'; interface DocumentElement { type: string; content: string; metadata?: Record<string, any>; confidence?: number; } interface DocumentMetadata { fileName: string; fileSize: number; format: string; elementCount: number; } interface DocumentDisplayProps { elements: DocumentElement[]; metadata: DocumentMetadata; className?: string; } export function DocumentDisplay({ elements, metadata, className }: DocumentDisplayProps) { const getConfidenceLevel = (confidence?: number) => { if (!confidence) return 'medium'; if (confidence >= 0.9) return 'high'; if (confidence >= 0.7) return 'medium'; return 'low'; }; const formatFileSize = (bytes: number) => { const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB']; let size = bytes; let unitIndex = 0; while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) { size /= 1024; unitIndex++; } return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`; }; return ( <Card className={cn("w-full", className)}> <CardHeader> <CardTitle>Document Content</CardTitle> <div className={metadataStyles({ layout: 'column', emphasis: 'high' })}> <div className="flex gap-2"> <Badge variant="outline">{metadata.format.toUpperCase()}</Badge> <Badge variant="outline">{formatFileSize(metadata.fileSize)}</Badge> <Badge variant="outline">{metadata.elementCount} elements</Badge> </div> <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{metadata.fileName}</span> </div> </CardHeader> <CardContent> <ScrollArea className="h-[600px] w-full rounded-md border"> <div className={documentContainerStyles()}> {elements.map((element, index) => ( <div key={index} className={documentStyles({ variant: element.type.toLowerCase() as any, confidence: getConfidenceLevel(element.confidence), className: 'transition-colors duration-200 hover:bg-muted/50 p-2 rounded' })} > <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-1"> <span className="text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground"> {element.type} </span> {element.confidence && ( <Badge variant="outline" className="text-xs"> {(element.confidence * 100).toFixed(0)}% confidence </Badge> )} </div> <div className="content">{element.content}</div> {element.metadata && ( <div className={metadataStyles({ emphasis: 'low' })}> {Object.entries(element.metadata).map(([key, value]) => ( <span key={key}> {key}: {value} </span> ))} </div> )} </div> ))} </div> </ScrollArea> </CardContent> </Card> ); }
```

# components\DocumentUpload.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import React, { useState } from 'react'; import { FilePond, registerPlugin } from 'react-filepond'; import 'filepond/dist/filepond.min.css'; import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from './ui/card'; import { DocumentDisplay } from './DocumentDisplay'; import { useToast } from '@/hooks/use-toast'; interface DocumentElement { type: string; content: string; metadata?: Record<string, any>; confidence?: number; } interface DocumentMetadata { fileName: string; fileSize: number; format: string; elementCount: number; } interface ProcessedResult { success: boolean; data: { elements: DocumentElement[]; metadata: DocumentMetadata; sourceFormat: string; }; } export default function DocumentUpload() { const [result, setResult] = useState<ProcessedResult | null>(null); const { toast } = useToast(); const handleProcessSuccess = (response: string): string => { try { const data = JSON.parse(response); setResult(data); toast({ title: "Document Processed", description: `Successfully processed ${data.data.metadata.elementCount} elements`, }); return 'success'; } catch (err) { console.error('Error parsing response:', err); toast({ title: "Processing Error", description: "Failed to parse server response", variant: "destructive", }); return 'error'; } }; const handleProcessError = (error: any) => { console.error('Upload error:', error); toast({ title: "Processing Failed", description: error.message || "Failed to process document", variant: "destructive", }); }; return ( <div className="space-y-6"> <Card> <CardHeader> <CardTitle>Document Upload</CardTitle> </CardHeader> <CardContent> <FilePond allowMultiple={false} maxFiles={1} acceptedFileTypes={['application/pdf', 'text/plain']} labelIdle='Drag & Drop your document or <span class="filepond--label-action">Browse</span>' server={{ process: { url: '/api/process-document', method: 'POST', onload: handleProcessSuccess, onerror: handleProcessError, headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json', }, }, }} styleButtonProcessItemPosition="right" styleButtonRemoveItemPosition="right" styleItemPanelAspectRatio="0.5" credits={false} className="filepond--root" /> </CardContent> </Card> {result && result.success && ( <DocumentDisplay elements={result.data.elements} metadata={result.data.metadata} className="animate-in fade-in-50 duration-500" /> )} </div> ); }
```

# components\DocumentViewer.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import React, { useState } from 'react'; import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card'; import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area'; import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button'; import { Upload } from 'lucide-react'; export default function DocumentViewer() { const [content, setContent] = useState<string | null>(null); const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false); const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null); async function handleFileUpload(e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) { const file = e.target.files?.[0]; if (!file) return; setLoading(true); setError(null); try { const formData = new FormData(); formData.append('file', file); const response = await fetch('/api/process-document', { method: 'POST', body: formData, }); if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed to process document'); const data = await response.json(); setContent(data.text); } catch (err) { setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Failed to process document'); } finally { setLoading(false); } } return ( <Card className="w-full"> <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between"> <CardTitle>Document Viewer</CardTitle> <div className="flex items-center gap-4"> <Button variant="outline" size="icon" asChild> <label> <Upload className="h-4 w-4" /> <input type="file" className="hidden" accept=".txt,.md" onChange={handleFileUpload} disabled={loading} /> </label> </Button> </div> </CardHeader> <CardContent> <ScrollArea className="h-[600px] w-full rounded-md border"> <div className="p-4"> {loading ? ( <div className="flex justify-center p-4"> <div className="text-muted-foreground">Processing...</div> </div> ) : error ? ( <div className="text-red-500 p-4">{error}</div> ) : content ? ( <pre className="whitespace-pre-wrap font-mono text-sm">{content}</pre> ) : ( <div className="text-center text-muted-foreground"> Upload a document to view its contents </div> )} </div> </ScrollArea> </CardContent> </Card> ); }
```

# components\MeetingDetails.tsx

```tsx
"use client" import React from "react" import { motion } from "framer-motion" import { ScrollArea } from "components/ui/scroll-area" import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "components/ui/card" import { Tabs, TabsContent, TabsList, TabsTrigger } from "components/ui/tabs" import { CheckCircle, Flag, AlertCircle, Lightbulb, Calendar, Users, List, AlertTriangle, FileText, Download, } from "lucide-react" import CategoryCard from "components/CategoryCard" import AudioTranscriptPlayer from "components/AudioTranscriptPlayer" import axios from "axios" import { useToast } from "hooks/use-toast" import type { TranscriptSegment, MeetingWithParsedFields } from "types/global" interface MeetingDetailsProps { data: MeetingWithParsedFields; } export default function MeetingDetails({ data }: MeetingDetailsProps) { const { toast } = useToast(); const [parsedTranscript, setParsedTranscript] = React.useState<string>(''); const [parsedSegments, setParsedSegments] = React.useState<TranscriptSegment[] | null>(null); // Parse transcript and segments from raw transcript React.useEffect(() => { try { if (typeof data.rawTranscript === 'string') { const parsed = JSON.parse(data.rawTranscript); // Set transcript text setParsedTranscript(parsed.text || ''); // Parse segments if available if (parsed.segments && Array.isArray(parsed.segments)) { const segments = parsed.segments.map((segment: any) => ({ text: segment.text.trim(), start: parseFloat(segment.start), end: parseFloat(segment.end), speaker: segment.speaker || '', words: Array.isArray(segment.words) ? segment.words.map((word: any) => ({ word: word.word, start: parseFloat(word.start), end: parseFloat(word.end), confidence: word.confidence || 1 })) : [] })); setParsedSegments(segments); console.log('Successfully parsed segments:', { count: segments.length, sample: segments.slice(0, 3) }); } else if (parsed.word_timestamps && Array.isArray(parsed.word_timestamps)) { // Fallback: Create segments from word timestamps const segments = createSegmentsFromWords(parsed.word_timestamps); setParsedSegments(segments); console.log('Created segments from word timestamps:', { count: segments.length, sample: segments.slice(0, 3) }); } } } catch (e) { console.error('Failed to parse transcript data:', e); setParsedTranscript(''); setParsedSegments(null); } }, [data.rawTranscript]); // Helper function to create segments from word timestamps const createSegmentsFromWords = (wordTimings: any[]): TranscriptSegment[] => { const segments: TranscriptSegment[] = []; let currentSegment: TranscriptSegment = { text: '', start: 0, end: 0, speaker: '', words: [] }; let words: string[] = []; wordTimings.forEach((timing, index) => { const word = timing.word.trim(); const isPunctuation = /[.!?]$/.test(word); words.push(word); if (index === 0) { currentSegment.start = parseFloat(timing.start); } if (isPunctuation || index === wordTimings.length - 1) { currentSegment.text = words.join(' '); currentSegment.end = parseFloat(timing.end); currentSegment.words = words.map((w, i) => ({ word: w, start: parseFloat(wordTimings[index - words.length + i + 1].start), end: parseFloat(wordTimings[index - words.length + i + 1].end), confidence: wordTimings[index - words.length + i + 1].confidence || 1 })); segments.push({ ...currentSegment }); // Reset for next segment currentSegment = { text: '', start: parseFloat(timing.end), end: 0, speaker: '', words: [] }; words = []; } }); return segments; }; // Debug log for meeting data React.useEffect(() => { console.log('Meeting data structure:', { hasAudioFile: !!data.audioFile, audioFilePath: data.audioFile, hasSegments: !!parsedSegments, segmentsType: typeof parsedSegments, segmentsLength: parsedSegments?.length, segmentsSample: parsedSegments?.slice(0, 3), rawTranscriptType: typeof data.rawTranscript, rawTranscriptLength: data.rawTranscript?.length, parsedTranscriptLength: parsedTranscript?.length }); }, [data, parsedTranscript, parsedSegments]); const categories = [ { title: "Tasks", icon: CheckCircle, items: data.breakdown.Tasks || [], gridSpan: "col-span-2", }, { title: "Decisions", icon: Flag, items: data.breakdown.Decisions || [], gridSpan: "col-span-2", }, { title: "Questions", icon: AlertCircle, items: data.breakdown.Questions || [], gridSpan: "col-span-2", }, { title: "Insights", icon: Lightbulb, items: data.breakdown.Insights || [], gridSpan: "col-span-2", }, { title: "Deadlines", icon: Calendar, items: data.breakdown.Deadlines || [], gridSpan: "col-span-1", }, { title: "Attendees", icon: Users, items: data.breakdown.Attendees || [], gridSpan: "col-span-1", }, { title: "Follow-ups", icon: List, items: data.breakdown["Follow-ups"] || [], gridSpan: "col-span-2", }, { title: "Risks", icon: AlertTriangle, items: data.breakdown.Risks || [], gridSpan: "col-span-2", }, ]; const handleExport = async () => { try { const response = await axios.get(`/api/meetings/${data.id}/export`, { responseType: 'blob', }); if (response.status === 200) { const url = window.URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([response.data])); const link = document.createElement('a'); link.href = url; link.setAttribute('download', `${data.name.replace(/\s+/g, '_')}_Details.docx`); document.body.appendChild(link); link.click(); link.parentNode?.removeChild(link); toast({ title: "Success", description: "Meeting details exported successfully!", }); } } catch (error: any) { console.error(error); toast({ title: "Error", description: "Failed to export meeting details.", variant: "destructive", }); } }; return ( <div className="container mx-auto p-6 bg-background pb-24"> <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-4"> <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold">{data.name}</h1> <button onClick={handleExport} className="flex items-center px-4 py-2 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded hover:bg-blue-700" > <Download className="w-5 h-5 mr-2" /> Export as DOCX </button> </div> <p className="text-muted-foreground mb-6">{data.description}</p> {/* Audio Player */} {data.audioFile && ( <div className="mb-6"> <AudioTranscriptPlayer audioUrl={data.audioFile} segments={parsedSegments} transcript={parsedTranscript} /> </div> )} <Tabs defaultValue="summary"> <TabsList className="mb-4"> <TabsTrigger value="summary">Summary</TabsTrigger> <TabsTrigger value="details">Details</TabsTrigger> </TabsList> <TabsContent value="summary"> <div className="space-y-6"> <Card> <CardHeader> <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2"> <FileText className="w-5 h-5" /> <span>Summary</span> </CardTitle> </CardHeader> <CardContent> <p>{data.summary}</p> </CardContent> </Card> <Card> <CardHeader> <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2"> <FileText className="w-5 h-5" /> <span>Transcript</span> </CardTitle> </CardHeader> <CardContent> <div className="prose prose-sm max-w-none"> <p className="whitespace-pre-wrap leading-relaxed"> {parsedTranscript} </p> </div> </CardContent> </Card> </div> </TabsContent> <TabsContent value="details"> <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-6"> {categories.map((category, index) => ( <motion.div key={category.title} className={category.gridSpan} initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ duration: 0.5, delay: index * 0.1 }} > <CategoryCard title={category.title} items={category.items} gridSpan={category.gridSpan} /> </motion.div> ))} </div> </TabsContent> </Tabs> </div> ); }
```

# components\test\AnalysisDisplay.tsx

```tsx
import React from 'react'; import { ScrollArea } from 'components/ui/scroll-area'; import { Card, CardHeader, CardTitle, CardContent } from 'components/ui/card'; interface AnalysisResult { Breakdown: { tasks: Array<{ description: string; assigned_to: string; priority: string; }>; decisions: Array<{ description: string; }>; questions: Array<{ question: string; raised_by: string; status: string; answer?: string; }>; insights: Array<{ description: string; }>; deadlines: Array<{ description: string; date: string; }>; attendees: Array<{ name: string; role: string; }>; follow_ups: Array<{ description: string; owner: string; due_date: string; }>; risks: Array<{ description: string; impact: string; }>; agenda: Array<string>; meeting_name: string; description: string; summary: string; }; } export function AnalysisDisplay({ analysis, }: { analysis: AnalysisResult['Breakdown']; }) { if (!analysis) { return ( <Card className="w-full"> <CardContent className="p-6"> <p className="text-muted-foreground text-center">No analysis data available</p> </CardContent> </Card> ); } return ( <Card className="w-full"> <CardHeader> <CardTitle>{analysis.meeting_name || 'Analysis Results'}</CardTitle> </CardHeader> <CardContent> <ScrollArea className="h-[70vh] w-full rounded-md border p-4"> <div className="space-y-8"> {/* Description Section */} {analysis.description && ( <section> <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">Description</h3> <p className="text-muted-foreground">{analysis.description}</p> </section> )} {/* Summary Section */} {analysis.summary && ( <section> <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">Summary</h3> <p className="text-muted-foreground">{analysis.summary}</p> </section> )} {/* Agenda Section */} {analysis.agenda?.length > 0 && ( <section> <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-3">Agenda</h3> <ul className="list-disc pl-6 space-y-2"> {analysis.agenda.map((item, index) => ( <li key={index} className="text-muted-foreground">{item}</li> ))} </ul> </section> )} {/* Tasks Section */} {analysis.tasks?.length > 0 && ( <section> <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-3">Tasks</h3> <div className="space-y-2"> {analysis.tasks.map((task, index) => ( <div key={index} className="bg-muted p-4 rounded-lg"> <p className="font-medium">{task.description}</p> <div className="mt-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground flex gap-4"> <span>Assigned to: {task.assigned_to}</span> <span>Priority: {task.priority}</span> </div> </div> ))} </div> </section> )} {/* Decisions Section */} {analysis.decisions?.length > 0 && ( <section> <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-3">Decisions</h3> <div className="space-y-2"> {analysis.decisions.map((decision, index) => ( <div key={index} className="bg-muted p-4 rounded-lg"> <p className="font-medium">{decision.description}</p> </div> ))} </div> </section> )} {/* Questions Section */} {analysis.questions?.length > 0 && ( <section> <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-3">Questions</h3> <div className="space-y-2"> {analysis.questions.map((question, index) => ( <div key={index} className="bg-muted p-4 rounded-lg"> <p className="font-medium">Q: {question.question}</p> <div className="mt-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground"> <p>Status: {question.status}</p> {question.answer && <p className="mt-1">A: {question.answer}</p>} </div> </div> ))} </div> </section> )} {/* Insights Section */} {analysis.insights?.length > 0 && ( <section> <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-3">Insights</h3> <div className="space-y-2"> {analysis.insights.map((insight, index) => ( <div key={index} className="bg-muted p-4 rounded-lg"> <p className="font-medium">{insight.description}</p> </div> ))} </div> </section> )} {/* Deadlines Section */} {analysis.deadlines?.length > 0 && ( <section> <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-3">Deadlines</h3> <div className="space-y-2"> {analysis.deadlines.map((deadline, index) => ( <div key={index} className="bg-muted p-4 rounded-lg"> <p className="font-medium">{deadline.description}</p> <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground">Due: {deadline.date}</p> </div> ))} </div> </section> )} {/* Attendees Section */} {analysis.attendees?.length > 0 && ( <section> <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-3">Attendees</h3> <div className="space-y-2"> {analysis.attendees.map((attendee, index) => ( <div key={index} className="bg-muted p-4 rounded-lg"> <p className="font-medium">{attendee.name}</p> <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Role: {attendee.role}</p> </div> ))} </div> </section> )} {/* Follow-ups Section */} {analysis.follow_ups?.length > 0 && ( <section> <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-3">Follow-ups</h3> <div className="space-y-2"> {analysis.follow_ups.map((followUp, index) => ( <div key={index} className="bg-muted p-4 rounded-lg"> <p className="font-medium">{followUp.description}</p> <div className="mt-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground flex gap-4"> <span>Owner: {followUp.owner}</span> <span>Due: {followUp.due_date}</span> </div> </div> ))} </div> </section> )} {/* Risks Section */} {analysis.risks?.length > 0 && ( <section> <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-3">Risks</h3> <div className="space-y-2"> {analysis.risks.map((risk, index) => ( <div key={index} className="bg-muted p-4 rounded-lg"> <p className="font-medium">{risk.description}</p> <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground">Impact: {risk.impact}</p> </div> ))} </div> </section> )} </div> </ScrollArea> </CardContent> </Card> ); } export default AnalysisDisplay;
```

# components\test\AudioCompressor.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import React, { useState } from 'react'; import { Button } from '../ui/button'; import { Card, CardHeader, CardTitle, CardContent } from '../ui/card'; import { useToast } from '../../hooks/use-toast'; import { FFmpeg } from '@ffmpeg/ffmpeg'; import { fetchFile } from '@ffmpeg/util'; // Initialize ffmpeg lazily only when needed let ffmpeg: FFmpeg | null = null; interface AudioCompressorProps { file: File | null; onCompressionComplete: (compressedFile: File) => void; } export function AudioCompressor({ file, onCompressionComplete }: AudioCompressorProps) { const [isCompressing, setIsCompressing] = useState(false); const { toast } = useToast(); const loadFFmpeg = async () => { if (!ffmpeg) { ffmpeg = new FFmpeg(); } if (!ffmpeg.loaded) { await ffmpeg.load(); } }; const compressAudio = async () => { if (!file) return; setIsCompressing(true); try { await loadFFmpeg(); if (!ffmpeg) throw new Error('FFmpeg not initialized'); await ffmpeg.writeFile('input_audio', await fetchFile(file)); await ffmpeg.exec([ '-i', 'input_audio', '-ar', '16000', '-ac', '1', '-b:a', '16k', 'output_audio.mp3' ]); const data = await ffmpeg.readFile('output_audio.mp3'); const compressedBlob = new Blob([data], { type: 'audio/mpeg' }); const compressed = new File([compressedBlob], `compressed_${file.name}`, { type: 'audio/mpeg', }); onCompressionComplete(compressed); toast({ title: 'Compression Successful', description: `File size reduced to ${(compressed.size / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(2)} MB`, }); } catch (error) { console.error('Compression error:', error); toast({ title: 'Compression Failed', description: 'An error occurred while compressing the audio.', variant: 'destructive', }); } finally { setIsCompressing(false); } }; const getFileSizeMB = (file: File | null): number => { return file ? file.size / (1024 ** 2) : 0; }; const isCompressionNeeded = file && getFileSizeMB(file) > 24; if (!isCompressionNeeded) return null; return ( <Card> <CardHeader> <CardTitle>Audio Compression</CardTitle> </CardHeader> <CardContent> <div className="space-y-4"> <p>File size: {getFileSizeMB(file).toFixed(2)} MB</p> <Button onClick={compressAudio} disabled={isCompressing}> {isCompressing ? 'Compressing...' : 'Compress Audio'} </Button> <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground"> File size exceeds 24 MB. Compression is recommended for better performance. </p> </div> </CardContent> </Card> ); }
```

# components\test\FileSelector.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react'; import { Button } from '../ui/button'; import { Input } from '../ui/input'; import { Label } from '../ui/label'; import { Card, CardHeader, CardTitle, CardContent, CardDescription } from '../ui/card'; import { useToast } from '../../hooks/use-toast'; interface MonitoredFile { name: string; size: number; lastModified: string; } interface FileSelectorProps { onFileSelect: (file: File) => void; disabled?: boolean; } export function FileSelector({ onFileSelect, disabled }: FileSelectorProps) { const [monitoredFiles, setMonitoredFiles] = useState<MonitoredFile[]>([]); const { toast } = useToast(); useEffect(() => { fetchMonitoredFiles(); const interval = setInterval(fetchMonitoredFiles, 10000); // Poll every 10 seconds return () => clearInterval(interval); }, []); const fetchMonitoredFiles = async () => { try { const response = await fetch('/api/monitored-files'); if (response.ok) { const files: MonitoredFile[] = await response.json(); setMonitoredFiles(files); } } catch (error) { console.error('Error fetching monitored files:', error); } }; const handleFileChange = (event: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => { const file = event.target.files?.[0]; if (file) { if (file.size > 25 * 1024 * 1024) { toast({ title: 'File too large', description: 'Please select a file smaller than 25MB', variant: 'destructive', }); return; } onFileSelect(file); } }; const handleMonitoredFileSelect = async (fileName: string) => { try { const response = await fetch(`/api/monitored-files/${encodeURIComponent(fileName)}`); if (response.ok) { const blob = await response.blob(); const file = new File([blob], fileName, { type: blob.type }); onFileSelect(file); } } catch (error) { console.error('Error selecting monitored file:', error); toast({ title: 'File Selection Failed', description: 'An error occurred while selecting the file.', variant: 'destructive', }); } }; return ( <Card> <CardHeader> <CardTitle>Select Audio File</CardTitle> <CardDescription>Upload a new file or select from monitored files</CardDescription> </CardHeader> <CardContent> <div className="flex flex-col gap-4"> <div> <Label htmlFor="audio-file">Upload Audio File</Label> <Input id="audio-file" type="file" accept="audio/*" onChange={handleFileChange} disabled={disabled} onClick={(e) => (e.target as HTMLInputElement).value = ''} /> </div> {monitoredFiles.length > 0 && ( <div> <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">Monitored Files:</h3> <ul className="space-y-2"> {monitoredFiles.map((file) => ( <li key={file.name} className="flex items-center justify-between"> <span>{file.name} ({(file.size / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(2)} MB)</span> <Button onClick={() => handleMonitoredFileSelect(file.name)} disabled={disabled} > Select </Button> </li> ))} </ul> </div> )} </div> </CardContent> </Card> ); }
```

```tsx
// components/ui/alert.tsx import * as React from "react" import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority" import { cn } from "@/lib/utils" const alertVariants = cva( "relative w-full rounded-lg border px-4 py-3 text-sm [&>svg+div]:translate-y-[-3px] [&>svg]:absolute [&>svg]:left-4 [&>svg]:top-4 [&>svg]:text-foreground [&>svg~*]:pl-7", { variants: { variant: { default: "bg-background text-foreground", destructive: "border-destructive/50 text-destructive dark:border-destructive [&>svg]:text-destructive", }, }, defaultVariants: { variant: "default", }, } ) const Alert = React.forwardRef< HTMLDivElement, React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement> & VariantProps<typeof alertVariants> >(({ className, variant, ...props }, ref) => ( <div ref={ref} role="alert" className={cn(alertVariants({ variant }), className)} {...props} /> )) Alert.displayName = "Alert" const AlertTitle = React.forwardRef< HTMLParagraphElement, React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLHeadingElement> >(({ className, ...props }, ref) => ( <h5 ref={ref} className={cn("mb-1 font-medium leading-none tracking-tight", className)} {...props} /> )) AlertTitle.displayName = "AlertTitle" const AlertDescription = React.forwardRef< HTMLParagraphElement, React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLParagraphElement> >(({ className, ...props }, ref) => ( <div ref={ref} className={cn("text-sm [&_p]:leading-relaxed", className)} {...props} /> )) AlertDescription.displayName = "AlertDescription" export { Alert, AlertTitle, AlertDescription }
```

```tsx
// components/ui/dialog.tsx "use client" import * as React from "react" import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog" import { X } from "lucide-react" import { cn } from "@/lib/utils" const Dialog = DialogPrimitive.Root const DialogTrigger = DialogPrimitive.Trigger const DialogPortal = DialogPrimitive.Portal const DialogOverlay = React.forwardRef< React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>, React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay> >(({ className, ...props }, ref) => ( <DialogPrimitive.Overlay ref={ref} className={cn( "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/50 backdrop-blur-sm data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0", className )} {...props} /> )) DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.displayName const DialogContent = React.forwardRef< React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>, React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content> >(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => ( <DialogPortal> <DialogOverlay /> <DialogPrimitive.Content ref={ref} className={cn( "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left-1/2 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top-[48%] data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left-1/2 data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top-[48%] sm:rounded-lg", className )} {...props} > {children} <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground"> <X className="h-4 w-4" /> <span className="sr-only">Close</span> </DialogPrimitive.Close> </DialogPrimitive.Content> </DialogPortal> )) DialogContent.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Content.displayName const DialogHeader = ({ className, ...props }: React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>) => ( <div className={cn( "flex # components\ui\toaster.tsx
```

```tsx
"use client" import { Toast, ToastClose, ToastDescription, ToastProvider, ToastTitle, ToastViewport, } from "../../components/ui/toast" import { useToast } from "../../hooks/use-toast" export function Toaster() { const { toasts } = useToast() return ( <ToastProvider> {toasts.map(function ({ id, title, description, action, ...props }) { return ( <Toast key={id} {...props}> <div className="grid gap-1"> {title && <ToastTitle>{title}</ToastTitle>} {description && ( <ToastDescription>{description}</ToastDescription> )} </div> {action} <ToastClose /> </Toast> ) })} <ToastViewport /> </ToastProvider> ) }
```

# components\UploadAudio.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react'; import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button"; import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input"; import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label"; import { Card, CardHeader, CardTitle, CardContent, CardDescription } from "@/components/ui/card"; import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast"; import { FFmpeg } from '@ffmpeg/ffmpeg'; import { fetchFile } from '@ffmpeg/util'; // Initialize ffmpeg lazily only when needed let ffmpeg: FFmpeg | null = null; interface MonitoredFile { name: string; size: number; lastModified: string; } const UploadAudio: React.FC<{ onUploadSuccess: () => void }> = ({ onUploadSuccess }) => { const [selectedFile, setSelectedFile] = useState<File | null>(null); const [isCompressing, setIsCompressing] = useState(false); const [isTranscribing, setIsTranscribing] = useState(false); const [compressedFile, setCompressedFile] = useState<File | null>(null); const [monitoredFiles, setMonitoredFiles] = useState<MonitoredFile[]>([]); const { toast } = useToast(); useEffect(() => { fetchMonitoredFiles(); const interval = setInterval(fetchMonitoredFiles, 10000); // Poll every 10 seconds return () => clearInterval(interval); }, []); const fetchMonitoredFiles = async () => { try { const response = await fetch('/api/monitored-files'); if (response.ok) { const files: MonitoredFile[] = await response.json(); setMonitoredFiles(files); } } catch (error) { console.error('Error fetching monitored files:', error); } }; const handleFileChange = (event: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => { const file = event.target.files?.[0]; if (file) { setSelectedFile(file); setCompressedFile(null); } }; const handleMonitoredFileSelect = async (fileName: string) => { try { const response = await fetch(`/api/monitored-files/${encodeURIComponent(fileName)}`); if (response.ok) { const blob = await response.blob(); const file = new File([blob], fileName, { type: blob.type }); setSelectedFile(file); setCompressedFile(null); } } catch (error) { console.error('Error selecting monitored file:', error); toast({ title: 'File Selection Failed', description: 'An error occurred while selecting the file.', variant: 'destructive', }); } }; const loadFFmpeg = async () => { if (!ffmpeg) { ffmpeg = new FFmpeg(); } if (!ffmpeg.loaded) { await ffmpeg.load(); } }; const compressAudio = async () => { if (!selectedFile) return; setIsCompressing(true); try { await loadFFmpeg(); if (!ffmpeg) throw new Error('FFmpeg not initialized'); await ffmpeg.writeFile('input_audio', await fetchFile(selectedFile)); // Set target bitrate to reduce file size // Adjust parameters as needed await ffmpeg.exec([ '-i', 'input_audio', '-ar', '16000', '-ac', '1', '-b:a', '16k', 'output_audio.mp3' ]); const data = await ffmpeg.readFile('output_audio.mp3'); const compressedBlob = new Blob([data], { type: 'audio/mpeg' }); const compressed = new File([compressedBlob], `compressed_${selectedFile.name}`, { type: 'audio/mpeg', }); setCompressedFile(compressed); toast({ title: 'Compression Successful', description: `File size reduced to ${(compressed.size / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(2)} MB`, }); } catch (error) { console.error('Compression error:', error); toast({ title: 'Compression Failed', description: 'An error occurred while compressing the audio.', variant: 'destructive', }); } finally { setIsCompressing(false); } }; const handleTranscribe = async () => { const fileToUpload = compressedFile || selectedFile; if (!fileToUpload) return; setIsTranscribing(true); const formData = new FormData(); formData.append('audio', fileToUpload); formData.append('fullPath', fileToUpload.name); try { await fetch('/api/transcribe', { method: 'POST', body: formData, }); toast({ title: 'Transcription Started', description: 'Your audio is being transcribed.', }); onUploadSuccess(); } catch (error) { console.error('Transcription error:', error); toast({ title: 'Transcription Failed', description: 'An error occurred while transcribing the audio.', variant: 'destructive', }); } finally { setIsTranscribing(false); setSelectedFile(null); setCompressedFile(null); } }; const getFileSizeMB = (file: File | null): number => { return file ? file.size / (1024 ** 2) : 0; }; const isCompressionNeeded = selectedFile && getFileSizeMB(selectedFile) > 24; const isTranscribeDisabled = (selectedFile && getFileSizeMB(selectedFile) > 24 && (!compressedFile || getFileSizeMB(compressedFile) > 24)) || isCompressing || isTranscribing; return ( <Card> <CardHeader> <CardTitle>Upload New Audio</CardTitle> <CardDescription>Select an audio file to transcribe</CardDescription> </CardHeader> <CardContent> <div className="flex flex-col gap-4"> <Label htmlFor="audio-file">Audio File</Label> <Input id="audio-file" type="file" accept="audio/*" onChange={handleFileChange} /> {selectedFile && ( <p>Selected File: {selectedFile.name} ({getFileSizeMB(selectedFile).toFixed(2)} MB)</p> )} {monitoredFiles.length > 0 && ( <div> <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">Monitored Files:</h3> <ul className="space-y-2"> {monitoredFiles.map((file) => ( <li key={file.name} className="flex items-center justify-between"> <span>{file.name} ({(file.size / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(2)} MB)</span> <Button onClick={() => handleMonitoredFileSelect(file.name)}>Select</Button> </li> ))} </ul> </div> )} {isCompressionNeeded && ( <Button onClick={compressAudio} disabled={isCompressing}> {isCompressing ? 'Compressing...' : 'Compress Audio'} </Button> )} {compressedFile && ( <p>Compressed File: {compressedFile.name} ({getFileSizeMB(compressedFile).toFixed(2)} MB)</p> )} <Button onClick={handleTranscribe} disabled={isTranscribeDisabled}> {isTranscribing ? 'Transcribing...' : 'Transcribe Audio'} </Button> {isTranscribeDisabled && ( <p className="text-red-500"> {selectedFile && getFileSizeMB(compressedFile || selectedFile) > 24 ? 'File size exceeds 24 MB, please compress the file before transcribing.' : ''} </p> )} </div> </CardContent> </Card> ); }; export default UploadAudio;
```

```tsx
import React, { useState } from 'react'; import { Card, CardHeader, CardTitle, CardContent } from "@/components/ui/card"; import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button"; import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input"; import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label"; import { FileAudio, FileText } from 'lucide-react'; const UploadContent = ({ onUploadSuccess }: { onUploadSuccess: () => void }) => { const [file, setFile] = useState<File | null>(null); const [isProcessing, setIsProcessing] = useState(false); const handleFileChange = (event: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => { const selectedFile = event.target.files?.[0]; if (selectedFile) { setFile(selectedFile); } }; const processFile = async () => { if (!file) return; setIsProcessing(true); try { const formData = new FormData(); const endpoint = file.type === 'application/pdf' ? '/api/test-document' : '/api/test-transcribe'; if (file.type === 'application/pdf') { formData.append('file', file); } else { formData.append('audio', file); } const response = await fetch(endpoint, { method: 'POST', body: formData, }); if (!response.ok) { throw new Error('Failed to process file'); } onUploadSuccess(); setFile(null); } catch (error) { console.error('Error processing file:', error); } finally { setIsProcessing(false); } }; return ( <Card> <CardHeader> <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2"> {file?.type === 'application/pdf' ? ( <FileText className="h-6 w-6" /> ) : ( <FileAudio className="h-6 w-6" /> )} Upload Content </CardTitle> </CardHeader> <CardContent> <div className="flex flex-col gap-4"> <div className="grid w-full max-w-sm items-center gap-1.5"> <Label htmlFor="file">File</Label> <Input id="file" type="file" accept="audio/*,.pdf" onChange={handleFileChange} disabled={isProcessing} /> </div> {file && ( <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground"> Selected file: {file.name} ({(file.size / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(2)} MB) </div> )} <Button onClick={processFile} disabled={!file || isProcessing} className="w-full max-w-sm" > {isProcessing ? 'Processing...' : 'Process File'} </Button> </div> </CardContent> </Card> ); }; export default UploadContent;
```

# components\UploadModal.tsx

```tsx
import React, { useState } from 'react'; import { Dialog, DialogContent, DialogHeader, DialogTitle } from '@/components/ui/dialog'; import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button'; import { Alert, AlertTitle, AlertDescription } from '@/components/ui/alert'; import { FileUp, Upload, AlertCircle } from 'lucide-react'; import axios from 'axios'; const UploadModal = ({ onUploadSuccess }: { onUploadSuccess: () => void }) => { const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false); const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false); const [isProcessing, setIsProcessing] = useState(false); const [error, setError] = useState(''); const handleFileDrop = async (files: FileList) => { const file = files[0]; if (!file) return; if (file.size > 25 * 1024 * 1024) { setError('File size exceeds 25MB limit'); return; } const isAudio = file.type.startsWith('audio/'); const isPDF = file.type === 'application/pdf'; if (!isAudio && !isPDF) { setError('Only audio files and PDFs are supported'); return; } setError(''); setIsProcessing(true); const formData = new FormData(); formData.append('file', file); try { const response = await axios.post('/api/upload', formData); if (response.data.success) { onUploadSuccess(); setIsOpen(false); } else { setError(response.data.error || 'Failed to process file'); } } catch (error: any) { setError(error.response?.data?.error || 'Failed to process file'); } setIsProcessing(false); }; const handleDragOver = (e: React.DragEvent) => { e.preventDefault(); setIsDragging(true); }; const handleDragLeave = (e: React.DragEvent) => { e.preventDefault(); setIsDragging(false); }; const handleDrop = (e: React.DragEvent) => { e.preventDefault(); setIsDragging(false); handleFileDrop(e.dataTransfer.files); }; const handleFileSelect = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => { if (e.target.files) { handleFileDrop(e.target.files); } }; return ( <> <Button onClick={() => setIsOpen(true)} className="gap-2"> <Upload className="h-4 w-4" /> Upload </Button> <Dialog open={isOpen} onOpenChange={setIsOpen}> <DialogContent className="sm:max-w-md"> <DialogHeader> <DialogTitle>Upload Content</DialogTitle> </DialogHeader> <div className="grid gap-4"> <div className={`relative rounded-lg border-2 border-dashed p-12 text-center ${ isDragging ? 'border-blue-500 bg-blue-50' : 'border-gray-300' }`} onDragOver={handleDragOver} onDragLeave={handleDragLeave} onDrop={handleDrop} > <input type="file" className="absolute inset-0 w-full h-full opacity-0 cursor-pointer" accept="audio/*,.pdf" onChange={handleFileSelect} disabled={isProcessing} /> <FileUp className="mx-auto h-12 w-12 text-gray-400" /> <div className="mt-4"> <p className="text-sm font-semibold"> {isProcessing ? 'Processing...' : 'Drag and drop or click to upload'} </p> <p className="mt-1 text-xs text-gray-500"> Audio files or PDFs (max. 25MB) </p> </div> </div> {error && ( <Alert variant="destructive"> <AlertCircle className="h-4 w-4" /> <AlertTitle>Error</AlertTitle> <AlertDescription>{error}</AlertDescription> </Alert> )} </div> </DialogContent> </Dialog> </> ); }; export default UploadModal;
```

# docling-api\app\api\routes\document.py

```py
from fastapi import APIRouter, UploadFile, File, HTTPException
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
import shutil
from pathlib import Path
from ...core.config import settings
from ...core.logging import logger
from ...core.utils import get_safe_filepath
from ...services.document_processor import DocumentProcessor
from ...models.document import DocumentResponse

router = APIRouter()
processor = DocumentProcessor()

@router.post("/process", response_model=DocumentResponse)
async def process_document(file: UploadFile = File(...)) -> DocumentResponse:
    """
    Endpoint para processar documentos (PDF, DOCX, PPTX, HTML, imagens).
    
    Args:
        file: Arquivo para processamento
        
    Returns:
        DocumentResponse: Resultado do processamento do documento
        
    Raises:
        HTTPException: Se houver erro no upload ou processamento
    """
    # Garantir que o diretório de upload existe
    settings.UPLOAD_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    
    # Criar nome único para o arquivo
    temp_path = get_safe_filepath(settings.UPLOAD_DIR, f"temp_{file.filename}")
    
    try:
        logger.info(f"Recebendo arquivo: {file.filename}")
        
        # Salvar arquivo
        logger.debug(f"Salvando arquivo em: {temp_path}")
        with open(temp_path, "wb") as buffer:
            shutil.copyfileobj(file.file, buffer)
        
        # Processar documento usando docling
        result = await processor.process_file(temp_path)
        
        if not result.success:
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=500,
                detail=result.error or "Erro ao processar documento"
            )
            
        return result
            
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Erro no servidor: {str(e)}", exc_info=True)
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=500,
            detail=f"Erro no servidor: {str(e)}"
        )
        
    finally:
        # Limpar arquivo temporário
        if temp_path.exists():
            logger.debug(f"Removendo arquivo temporário: {temp_path}")
            temp_path.unlink()

@router.get("/health")
async def health_check() -> JSONResponse:
    """
    Endpoint para verificar a saúde da API.
    
    Returns:
        JSONResponse: Status da API
    """
    return JSONResponse(
        content={
            "status": "healthy",
            "version": settings.VERSION
        }
    )

```

# docling-api\app\core\config.py

```py
from pydantic_settings import BaseSettings
from functools import lru_cache
from pathlib import Path

class Settings(BaseSettings):
    # API Configuration
    API_V1_STR: str = "/api/v1"
    PROJECT_NAME: str = "Docling API"
    VERSION: str = "1.0.0"
    DESCRIPTION: str = "API para processamento de documentos PDF"
    ENVIRONMENT: str = "development"

    # CORS Configuration
    BACKEND_CORS_ORIGINS: list[str] = ["http://localhost:3000"]
    
    # File Upload Configuration
    UPLOAD_DIR: Path = Path("temp_uploads")
    MAX_UPLOAD_SIZE: int = 10 * 1024 * 1024  # 10MB
    ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS: set[str] = {"pdf"}
    
    # Logging Configuration
    LOG_LEVEL: str = "INFO"
    LOG_DIR: str = "logs"
    
    class Config:
        case_sensitive = True
        env_file = ".env"

@lru_cache()
def get_settings() -> Settings:
    """Retorna as configurações da aplicação (cached)."""
    return Settings()

# Criar instância das configurações
settings = get_settings()

# Garantir que o diretório de upload existe
settings.UPLOAD_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

```

# docling-api\app\core\logging.py

```py
import logging
import sys
from pathlib import Path
from logging.handlers import RotatingFileHandler
from .config import settings

# Criar diretório de logs se não existir
log_dir = Path("logs")
log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

# Configurar o formato do log
log_format = logging.Formatter(
    "%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s"
)

def setup_logger(name: str) -> logging.Logger:
    """
    Configura e retorna um logger com handlers para arquivo e console.
    
    Args:
        name: Nome do logger
        
    Returns:
        logging.Logger: Logger configurado
    """
    logger = logging.getLogger(name)
    logger.setLevel(getattr(logging, settings.LOG_LEVEL))

    # Handler para arquivo
    file_handler = RotatingFileHandler(
        log_dir / f"{name}.log",
        maxBytes=10485760,  # 10MB
        backupCount=5,
        encoding="utf-8"
    )
    file_handler.setFormatter(log_format)
    logger.addHandler(file_handler)

    # Handler para console
    console_handler = logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout)
    console_handler.setFormatter(log_format)
    logger.addHandler(console_handler)

    return logger

# Logger principal da aplicação
logger = setup_logger("docling")

```

# docling-api\app\core\utils.py

```py
import re
import unicodedata
from pathlib import Path

def sanitize_filename(filename: str) -> str:
    """
    Sanitiza um nome de arquivo para uso seguro em sistemas de arquivos.
    
    Args:
        filename: Nome do arquivo para sanitizar
        
    Returns:
        str: Nome do arquivo sanitizado
    """
    # Remover acentos
    filename = unicodedata.normalize('NFKD', filename).encode('ASCII', 'ignore').decode('ASCII')
    
    # Substituir caracteres especiais e espaços por underscore
    filename = re.sub(r'[^\w\-\.]', '_', filename)
    
    # Remover underscores múltiplos
    filename = re.sub(r'_+', '_', filename)
    
    return filename

def get_safe_filepath(base_dir: Path, filename: str) -> Path:
    """
    Cria um caminho de arquivo seguro combinando diretório base e nome de arquivo.
    
    Args:
        base_dir: Diretório base
        filename: Nome do arquivo original
        
    Returns:
        Path: Caminho completo e seguro para o arquivo
    """
    safe_name = sanitize_filename(filename)
    return base_dir.resolve() / safe_name

```

# docling-api\app\main.py

```py
from fastapi import FastAPI
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from .core.config import settings
from .core.logging import logger
from .api.routes import document

# Criar aplicação FastAPI
app = FastAPI(
    title=settings.PROJECT_NAME,
    version=settings.VERSION,
    description=settings.DESCRIPTION,
)

# Configurar CORS
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["http://localhost:3000"],
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
    expose_headers=["*"],
)

# Incluir rotas
app.include_router(
    document.router,
    prefix=f"{settings.API_V1_STR}/documents",
    tags=["documents"]
)

@app.on_event("startup")
async def startup_event():
    """Evento executado na inicialização da aplicação."""
    logger.info("Iniciando Docling API")
    
    # Garantir que o diretório de upload existe
    settings.UPLOAD_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    logger.info(f"Diretório de upload configurado: {settings.UPLOAD_DIR}")

@app.on_event("shutdown")
async def shutdown_event():
    """Evento executado no desligamento da aplicação."""
    logger.info("Encerrando Docling API")

# Rota raiz
@app.get("/")
async def root():
    """Rota raiz da API."""
    return {
        "name": settings.PROJECT_NAME,
        "version": settings.VERSION,
        "description": settings.DESCRIPTION
    }
```

# docling-api\app\models\document.py

```py
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Union
from pydantic import BaseModel
from enum import Enum

class DocumentItemType(str, Enum):
    TEXT = "text"
    TABLE = "table"
    HEADING = "heading"
    CAPTION = "caption"
    IMAGE = "image"

class TableData(BaseModel):
    headers: List[str]
    rows: List[List[str]]
    caption: Optional[str] = None

class DocumentItem(BaseModel):
    type: DocumentItemType
    content: Union[str, TableData]
    level: int = 0
    metadata: Optional[Dict] = None

class DocumentMetadata(BaseModel):
    title: Optional[str] = None
    author: Optional[str] = None
    subject: Optional[str] = None
    keywords: Optional[str] = None
    pageCount: Optional[int] = None
    format: str
    processedAt: str

class DocumentResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response model for document processing."""
    success: bool
    items: List[DocumentItem]
    metadata: DocumentMetadata
    error: Optional[str] = None
    raw_text: Optional[str] = None

```

# docling-api\app\services\document_processor.py

```py
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime
from typing import List, Optional, Dict

from docling.document_converter import DocumentConverter
from docling.datamodel.base_models import InputFormat
from docling.datamodel.document import DoclingDocument
from docling.datamodel.items import TextItem, TableItem, ImageItem

from ..core.logging import logger
from ..models.document import (
    DocumentResponse,
    DocumentMetadata,
    DocumentItem,
    DocumentItemType,
    TableData,
)

class DocumentProcessor:
    def __init__(self):
        self.converter = DocumentConverter(
            allowed_formats=[
                InputFormat.PDF,
                InputFormat.DOCX,
                InputFormat.PPTX,
                InputFormat.HTML,
                InputFormat.IMAGE,
            ]
        )

    async def process_file(self, file_path: str | Path) -> DocumentResponse:
        """
        Processa um arquivo usando docling.
        
        Args:
            file_path: Caminho para o arquivo
            
        Returns:
            DocumentResponse: Resultado do processamento
        """
        try:
            logger.info(f"Iniciando processamento do arquivo: {file_path}")
            
            # Converter arquivo usando docling
            result = self.converter.convert(str(file_path))
            
            if not result.success:
                raise Exception(result.error or "Falha ao processar documento")
            
            # Extrair itens do documento
            items: List[DocumentItem] = []
            raw_text = ""
            
            # Processar o documento
            for item, level in result.document.iterate_items():
                if isinstance(item, TextItem):
                    # Texto pode incluir cabeçalhos e legendas
                    item_type = DocumentItemType.TEXT
                    if hasattr(item, 'is_heading') and item.is_heading:
                        item_type = DocumentItemType.HEADING
                    elif hasattr(item, 'is_caption') and item.is_caption:
                        item_type = DocumentItemType.CAPTION
                        
                    items.append(DocumentItem(
                        type=item_type,
                        content=item.text,
                        level=level,
                        metadata=item.metadata if hasattr(item, 'metadata') else None
                    ))
                    raw_text += item.text + "\n"
                    
                elif isinstance(item, TableItem):
                    df = item.export_to_dataframe()
                    items.append(DocumentItem(
                        type=DocumentItemType.TABLE,
                        content=TableData(
                            headers=df.columns.tolist(),
                            rows=df.values.tolist(),
                            caption=item.caption if hasattr(item, 'caption') else None
                        ),
                        level=level,
                        metadata=item.metadata if hasattr(item, 'metadata') else None
                    ))
                    
                elif isinstance(item, ImageItem):
                    metadata: Dict = {}
                    if hasattr(item, 'location'):
                        metadata['location'] = item.location
                    if hasattr(item, 'metadata'):
                        metadata.update(item.metadata)
                        
                    items.append(DocumentItem(
                        type=DocumentItemType.IMAGE,
                        content=item.caption if hasattr(item, 'caption') else "",
                        level=level,
                        metadata=metadata
                    ))
            
            # Criar metadata
            metadata = DocumentMetadata(
                title=result.document.metadata.get("title", ""),
                author=result.document.metadata.get("author", ""),
                subject=result.document.metadata.get("subject", ""),
                keywords=result.document.metadata.get("keywords", ""),
                pageCount=result.document.metadata.get("pageCount"),
                format=str(result.document.metadata.get("format", Path(file_path).suffix[1:])),
                processedAt=datetime.now().isoformat()
            )
            
            logger.info(f"Arquivo processado com sucesso: {file_path}")
            
            return DocumentResponse(
                success=True,
                items=items,
                metadata=metadata,
                raw_text=raw_text
            )
            
        except Exception as e:
            error_msg = f"Erro ao processar documento: {str(e)}"
            logger.error(error_msg, exc_info=True)
            return DocumentResponse(
                success=False,
                items=[],
                metadata=DocumentMetadata(
                    format=str(Path(file_path).suffix[1:]),
                    processedAt=datetime.now().isoformat()
                ),
                error=error_msg
            )

```

# docling-api\app\services\pdf_processor.py

```py
import fitz  # PyMuPDF
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, Any
from ..core.logging import logger
from ..core.utils import get_safe_filepath
from ..models.document import DocumentResponse, DocumentMetadata

class PDFProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    async def process_file(file_path: str | Path) -> DocumentResponse:
        """
        Processa um arquivo PDF e extrai texto e metadados.
        
        Args:
            file_path: Caminho para o arquivo PDF
            
        Returns:
            DocumentResponse: Resposta contendo texto e metadados do documento
        """
        doc = None
        try:
            # Usar utilitário para garantir caminho seguro
            file_path = Path(str(file_path))
            if not isinstance(file_path, Path):
                file_path = get_safe_filepath(file_path.parent, file_path.name)
            logger.info(f"Iniciando processamento do arquivo: {file_path}")
            
            # Verificar se o arquivo existe
            if not file_path.exists():
                raise FileNotFoundError(f"Arquivo não encontrado: {file_path}")
            
            # Abrir o PDF
            doc = fitz.open(str(file_path))
            
            # Extrair texto de todas as páginas
            text = ""
            for page in doc:
                text += page.get_text()
                
            # Obter metadados
            metadata = doc.metadata
            page_count = len(doc)
            
            logger.info(f"Arquivo processado com sucesso: {file_path}")
            
            return DocumentResponse(
                success=True,
                text=text,
                metadata=DocumentMetadata(
                    title=metadata.get("title", ""),
                    author=metadata.get("author", ""),
                    subject=metadata.get("subject", ""),
                    keywords=metadata.get("keywords", ""),
                    pageCount=page_count
                )
            )
            
        except Exception as e:
            error_msg = f"Erro ao processar PDF: {str(e)}"
            logger.error(error_msg, exc_info=True)
            return DocumentResponse(
                success=False,
                text="",
                error=error_msg
            )
            
        finally:
            if doc:
                doc.close()
                logger.debug(f"Documento fechado: {file_path}")

    @staticmethod
    def validate_pdf(file_path: str | Path) -> bool:
        """
        Valida se um arquivo é um PDF válido.
        
        Args:
            file_path: Caminho para o arquivo
            
        Returns:
            bool: True se o arquivo for um PDF válido, False caso contrário
        """
        try:
            # Usar utilitário para garantir caminho seguro
            file_path = Path(str(file_path))
            if not isinstance(file_path, Path):
                file_path = get_safe_filepath(file_path.parent, file_path.name)
            
            # Verificar se o arquivo existe
            if not file_path.exists():
                logger.warning(f"Arquivo não encontrado: {file_path}")
                return False
                
            with fitz.open(str(file_path)) as doc:
                # Tentar acessar a primeira página
                _ = doc[0]
                return True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Arquivo inválido: {file_path}. Erro: {str(e)}")
            return False

```

# docling-api\docker-compose.yml

```yml
version: '3.8'

services:
  docling-api:
    build: .
    ports:
      - "8000:8000"
    volumes:
      - ./app:/app/app
      - ./logs:/app/logs
      - ./temp_uploads:/app/temp_uploads
    environment:
      - ENVIRONMENT=development
      - MAX_UPLOAD_SIZE=10485760  # 10MB
      - LOG_LEVEL=INFO
    restart: unless-stopped
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/documents/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 10s

```

# docling-api\Dockerfile

```
# Usar imagem Python oficial como base FROM python:3.12-slim # Definir diretório de trabalho WORKDIR /app # Instalar dependências do sistema para PyMuPDF RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \ build-essential \ && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/* # Copiar requirements.txt COPY requirements.txt . # Instalar dependências Python RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt # Copiar código da aplicação COPY ./app ./app # Criar diretórios necessários RUN mkdir -p logs temp_uploads # Expor porta EXPOSE 8000 # Comando para executar a aplicação CMD ["uvicorn", "app.main:app", "--host", "0.0.0.0", "--port", "8000"]
```

# docling-api\README.md

```md
# Docling API API para processamento de documentos PDF com FastAPI e Docker. ## Funcionalidades - Upload e processamento de arquivos PDF - Extração de texto e metadados - Validação de arquivos - Logging configurável - Healthcheck endpoint - CORS configurável ## Requisitos - Python 3.12+ - Docker e Docker Compose - FastAPI - PyMuPDF ## Estrutura do Projeto \`\`\` docling-api/ ├── app/ │ ├── __init__.py │ ├── main.py # FastAPI app principal │ ├── core/ # Configurações e utilitários │ ├── api/ # Rotas da API │ ├── services/ # Lógica de negócios │ └── models/ # Modelos Pydantic ├── tests/ # Testes ├── Dockerfile ├── docker-compose.yml ├── requirements.txt └── README.md \`\`\` ## Configuração 1. Clone o repositório 2. Copie `.env.example` para `.env` e ajuste as configurações 3. Instale as dependências: \`\`\`bash pip install -r requirements.txt \`\`\` ## Execução Local \`\`\`bash uvicorn app.main:app --reload \`\`\` ## Execução com Docker \`\`\`bash docker-compose up --build \`\`\` ## Endpoints ### POST /api/v1/documents/process-pdf Processa um arquivo PDF e retorna texto e metadados. **Request:** - Método: POST - Content-Type: multipart/form-data - Body: arquivo PDF (campo: file) **Response:** \`\`\`json { "success": true, "text": "Conteúdo do PDF...", "metadata": { "title": "Título do documento", "author": "Autor", "subject": "Assunto", "keywords": "palavras-chave", "pageCount": 1 } } \`\`\` ### GET /api/v1/documents/health Verifica o status da API. **Response:** \`\`\`json { "status": "healthy", "version": "1.0.0" } \`\`\` ## Desenvolvimento 1. Crie um ambiente virtual: \`\`\`bash python -m venv venv source venv/bin/activate # Linux/Mac .\venv\Scripts\activate # Windows \`\`\` 2. Instale as dependências de desenvolvimento: \`\`\`bash pip install -r requirements.txt \`\`\` 3. Execute os testes: \`\`\`bash pytest \`\`\` ## Logs Os logs são armazenados em: - Console (stdout) - Arquivo rotativo em `logs/docling.log` ## Contribuição 1. Fork o repositório 2. Crie uma branch para sua feature 3. Commit suas mudanças 4. Push para a branch 5. Abra um Pull Request ## Licença MIT
```

