# docs\API.md

```md
# MeetingMind API Documentation ## Authentication All API endpoints except the landing page require authentication. Use NextAuth.js session tokens for requests. ## Base URL \`\`\` /api \`\`\` ## Endpoints ### Authentication \`\`\` POST /auth/[...nextauth] \`\`\` Handles all authentication flows through NextAuth.js. ### Transcription \`\`\` POST /transcribe \`\`\` **Request Body:** \`\`\`typescript { audio: File, fullPath: string } \`\`\` **Response:** \`\`\`typescript { id: string, name: string, description: string, rawTranscript: string, summary: string, audioFile: string, // ... related entities } \`\`\` ### Meetings #### List Meetings \`\`\` GET /meetings \`\`\` **Response:** \`\`\`typescript { meetings: Array<{ id: string, name: string, description: string, createdAt: string, updatedAt: string }> } \`\`\` #### Get Meeting \`\`\` GET /meetings/{id} \`\`\` **Response:** \`\`\`typescript { id: string, name: string, description: string, rawTranscript: string, summary: string, audioFile: string, tasks: Task[], decisions: Decision[], questions: Question[], insights: Insight[], deadlines: Deadline[], attendees: Attendee[], followUps: FollowUp[], risks: Risk[], agenda: AgendaItem[] } \`\`\` #### Create Meeting \`\`\` POST /meetings \`\`\` **Request Body:** \`\`\`typescript { name: string, description: string, audioFile?: string } \`\`\` #### Update Meeting \`\`\` PUT /meetings/{id} \`\`\` **Request Body:** \`\`\`typescript { name?: string, description?: string, summary?: string } \`\`\` #### Delete Meeting \`\`\` DELETE /meetings/{id} \`\`\` #### Export Meeting \`\`\` GET /meetings/{id}/export \`\`\` **Query Parameters:** \`\`\`typescript { format: 'docx' | 'pdf' | 'json' } \`\`\` ## Data Types ### Task \`\`\`typescript { id: string, task: string, owner: string, dueDate?: Date, meetingId: string, createdAt: Date, updatedAt: Date } \`\`\` ### Decision \`\`\`typescript { id: string, decision: string, date: Date, meetingId: string, createdAt: Date, updatedAt: Date } \`\`\` ### Question \`\`\`typescript { id: string, question: string, status: string, answer?: string, meetingId: string, createdAt: Date, updatedAt: Date } \`\`\` ### Insight \`\`\`typescript { id: string, insight: string, reference: string, meetingId: string, createdAt: Date, updatedAt: Date } \`\`\` ### Deadline \`\`\`typescript { id: string, description: string, dueDate?: Date, meetingId: string, createdAt: Date, updatedAt: Date } \`\`\` ### Attendee \`\`\`typescript { id: string, name: string, role: string, meetingId: string, createdAt: Date, updatedAt: Date } \`\`\` ### FollowUp \`\`\`typescript { id: string, description: string, owner: string, meetingId: string, createdAt: Date, updatedAt: Date } \`\`\` ### Risk \`\`\`typescript { id: string, risk: string, impact: string, meetingId: string, createdAt: Date, updatedAt: Date } \`\`\` ### AgendaItem \`\`\`typescript { id: string, item: string, meetingId: string, createdAt: Date, updatedAt: Date } \`\`\` ## Error Responses All endpoints may return the following error responses: ### 401 Unauthorized \`\`\`json { "error": "Authentication required." } \`\`\` ### 404 Not Found \`\`\`json { "error": "Resource not found." } \`\`\` ### 500 Internal Server Error \`\`\`json { "error": "An error occurred during processing." } \`\`\` ## Rate Limiting API endpoints are subject to rate limiting: - 100 requests per minute per IP - 1000 requests per hour per user ## File Upload Limits - Maximum audio file size: 100MB - Supported formats: MP3, WAV, M4A ## Security Considerations 1. **Authentication** - All requests must include a valid session token - Tokens are managed by NextAuth.js - Session expiration is enforced 2. **File Upload Security** - File type validation - Size limits - Malware scanning - Secure storage 3. **Data Access** - User-specific data isolation - Role-based access control - Input validation - Output sanitization ## Best Practices 1. **Rate Limiting** - Implement exponential backoff - Handle rate limit errors gracefully - Cache responses when possible 2. **Error Handling** - Use appropriate HTTP status codes - Provide meaningful error messages - Log errors for debugging 3. **Performance** - Minimize payload sizes - Use pagination for large datasets - Implement caching strategies ## Versioning The API follows semantic versioning. The current version is v1.0.0. Future versions will be accessible via URL versioning: \`\`\` /api/v2/... \`\`\` ## Support For API support and issues: 1. Check the documentation 2. Review common issues 3. Contact support team
```

# docs\ARCHITECTURE.md

```md
# MeetingMind Technical Architecture ## System Components ### 1. Frontend Layer \`\`\`mermaid graph LR A[Landing Page] --> B[Authentication] B --> C[Dashboard] C --> D[Meeting Upload] C --> E[Meeting Details] C --> F[Audio Player] \`\`\` ### 2. API Layer \`\`\`mermaid graph TD A[API Routes] --> B[/api/auth] A --> C[/api/transcribe] A --> D[/api/meetings] D --> E[CRUD Operations] D --> F[Export] \`\`\` ### 3. Data Flow \`\`\`mermaid graph TD A[Client] -->|Upload| B[API] B -->|Process| C[FFmpeg] C -->|Transcribe| D[AI Service] D -->|Analyze| E[Database] E -->|Serve| A \`\`\` ## Component Interactions ### Authentication Flow 1. User initiates sign-in 2. NextAuth handles provider authentication 3. Session created and stored 4. User redirected to dashboard ### Audio Processing Flow 1. Audio file uploaded to /api/transcribe 2. FFmpeg processes audio 3. File saved to uploads directory 4. Transcription service processes audio 5. AI analysis extracts meeting components 6. Structured data saved to database ### Meeting Management Flow 1. Meeting data stored in central Meeting entity 2. Related entities (tasks, decisions, etc.) linked 3. CRUD operations through /api/meetings 4. Real-time updates to UI ## Database Schema Relationships \`\`\`mermaid erDiagram User ||--o{ Meeting : owns Meeting ||--o{ Task : contains Meeting ||--o{ Decision : contains Meeting ||--o{ Question : contains Meeting ||--o{ Insight : contains Meeting ||--o{ Deadline : contains Meeting ||--o{ Attendee : has Meeting ||--o{ FollowUp : contains Meeting ||--o{ Risk : contains Meeting ||--o{ AgendaItem : contains \`\`\` ## Security Architecture ### Authentication Layer - NextAuth.js provider integration - Session management - JWT token handling - Prisma adapter integration ### Data Protection - Route protection middleware - User-specific data access - Secure file storage - Input validation ## Performance Considerations ### Optimization Strategies 1. Client-side caching 2. Efficient database queries 3. Chunked file uploads 4. Lazy loading components ### Scalability Points 1. Database connections 2. File storage system 3. API rate limiting 4. Processing queue management ## Error Handling ### Error Categories 1. Authentication errors 2. File processing errors 3. Database errors 4. API response errors ### Error Flow \`\`\`mermaid graph TD A[Error Occurs] --> B{Error Type} B -->|Auth| C[Auth Handler] B -->|API| D[API Handler] B -->|DB| E[DB Handler] C --> F[User Feedback] D --> F E --> F \`\`\` ## Deployment Architecture ### Production Environment 1. Next.js server 2. SQLite database 3. File storage system 4. Environment configuration ### Required Services 1. Authentication providers 2. AI transcription service 3. File processing service 4. Database management ## Monitoring and Logging ### Key Metrics 1. API response times 2. Processing durations 3. Error rates 4. Storage usage ### Log Categories 1. Access logs 2. Error logs 3. Performance logs 4. Security logs ## Future Considerations ### Scalability 1. Database migration path 2. Cloud storage integration 3. Processing queue implementation 4. Load balancing strategy ### Feature Expansion 1. Real-time collaboration 2. Advanced analytics 3. Integration capabilities 4. Export formats
```

# docs\README.md

```md
# MeetingMind Documentation ## Overview MeetingMind is a Next.js application that transforms audio recordings of meetings into structured, actionable insights using AI. The application provides transcription services, meeting analysis, and organized storage of meeting details. ## Tech Stack ### Core Technologies - **Frontend**: Next.js 14 with React 18 - **Backend**: Next.js API Routes - **Database**: SQLite with Prisma ORM - **Authentication**: NextAuth.js - **Styling**: Tailwind CSS - **Animation**: Framer Motion - **Audio Processing**: FFmpeg - **UI Components**: Radix UI ### Key Dependencies - `@prisma/client`: Database ORM - `@auth/prisma-adapter`: Authentication adapter for Prisma - `@ffmpeg/core`, `@ffmpeg/ffmpeg`: Audio processing - Various Radix UI components for accessible UI elements ## Architecture ### Database Schema #### Core Entities 1. **User** - Authentication and user management - Relations: One-to-many with Meetings 2. **Meeting** - Central entity storing meeting information - Fields: - name - description - rawTranscript - summary - audioFile - timestamps (createdAt, updatedAt) - Relations: One-to-many with various meeting components 3. **Meeting Components** - Tasks - Decisions - Questions - Insights - Deadlines - Attendees - Follow-ups - Risks - Agenda Items ### API Routes #### Authentication - `/api/auth/[...nextauth]`: Handles authentication flows #### Core Functionality - `/api/transcribe`: - Handles audio file upload - Processes transcription - Analyzes meeting content - Creates structured meeting data #### Meeting Management - `/api/meetings`: Meeting CRUD operations - `/api/meetings/[id]`: Individual meeting operations - `/api/meetings/[id]/export`: Meeting export functionality ## Features ### 1. Audio Processing - Supports audio file uploads - Uses FFmpeg for audio processing - Stores processed files in `/public/uploads` ### 2. Transcription & Analysis - Converts audio to text - AI-powered analysis of meeting content - Extracts key components: - Tasks and assignments - Decisions made - Questions raised - Key insights - Deadlines - Attendee information - Follow-up items - Risk assessments - Agenda items ### 3. User Interface - Responsive design - Modern gradient styling - Animated transitions - Accessible components - Dashboard for meeting management - Audio player component - Meeting details view ## Security ### Authentication - NextAuth.js implementation - Session-based authentication - Protected API routes - User-specific data access ### File Handling - Secure file upload processing - Controlled file access - Proper file storage management ## Development ### Environment Setup Required environment variables: \`\`\`env LANGFLOW_FLOW_URL=<API_URL> DATABASE_URL=<DB_URL> NEXTAUTH_SECRET=<SECRET> NEXTAUTH_URL=<AUTH_URL> \`\`\` ### Running the Application \`\`\`bash # Install dependencies npm install # Generate Prisma client npx prisma generate # Run development server npm run dev # Build for production npm run build # Start production server npm start \`\`\` ### Database Management \`\`\`bash # Open Prisma Studio npm run prisma:studio # Run migrations npx prisma migrate dev \`\`\` ## Project Structure \`\`\` ├── app/ │ ├── api/ # API routes │ ├── dashboard/ # Dashboard pages │ └── page.tsx # Landing page ├── components/ # React components │ ├── ui/ # UI components │ └── [feature]/ # Feature-specific components ├── lib/ # Shared utilities ├── prisma/ # Database schema and migrations ├── public/ # Static assets │ ├── uploads/ # Uploaded audio files │ └── monitored/ # Monitored files └── types/ # TypeScript type definitions \`\`\` ## Best Practices 1. **Code Organization** - Feature-based component structure - Separation of concerns - Type safety with TypeScript 2. **Security** - Authentication for all sensitive routes - Input validation - Secure file handling 3. **Performance** - Optimized file uploads - Efficient database queries - Client-side caching 4. **Error Handling** - Comprehensive error catching - User-friendly error messages - Proper error logging ## Deployment The application can be deployed to any platform that supports Next.js applications. Key considerations: 1. **Environment Variables** - Set all required environment variables - Configure authentication providers 2. **Database** - Run migrations - Configure database connection 3. **File Storage** - Configure upload directory - Set appropriate permissions 4. **SSL/TLS** - Enable HTTPS - Configure security headers
```

# hooks\use-toast.ts

```ts
// Inspired by react-hot-toast library import * as React from "react" import type { ToastActionElement, ToastProps, } from "../components/ui/toast" const TOAST_LIMIT = 1 const TOAST_REMOVE_DELAY = 1000000 type ToasterToast = ToastProps & { id: string title?: React.ReactNode description?: React.ReactNode action?: ToastActionElement } const actionTypes = { ADD_TOAST: "ADD_TOAST", UPDATE_TOAST: "UPDATE_TOAST", DISMISS_TOAST: "DISMISS_TOAST", REMOVE_TOAST: "REMOVE_TOAST", } as const let count = 0 function genId() { count = (count + 1) % Number.MAX_VALUE return count.toString() } type ActionType = typeof actionTypes type Action = | { type: ActionType["ADD_TOAST"] toast: ToasterToast } | { type: ActionType["UPDATE_TOAST"] toast: Partial<ToasterToast> } | { type: ActionType["DISMISS_TOAST"] toastId?: ToasterToast["id"] } | { type: ActionType["REMOVE_TOAST"] toastId?: ToasterToast["id"] } interface State { toasts: ToasterToast[] } const toastTimeouts = new Map<string, ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>>() const addToRemoveQueue = (toastId: string) => { if (toastTimeouts.has(toastId)) { return } const timeout = setTimeout(() => { toastTimeouts.delete(toastId) dispatch({ type: "REMOVE_TOAST", toastId: toastId, }) }, TOAST_REMOVE_DELAY) toastTimeouts.set(toastId, timeout) } export const reducer = (state: State, action: Action): State => { switch (action.type) { case "ADD_TOAST": return { ...state, toasts: [action.toast, ...state.toasts].slice(0, TOAST_LIMIT), } case "UPDATE_TOAST": return { ...state, toasts: state.toasts.map((t) => t.id === action.toast.id ? { ...t, ...action.toast } : t ), } case "DISMISS_TOAST": { const { toastId } = action // ! Side effects ! - This could be extracted into a dismissToast() action, // but I'll keep it here for simplicity if (toastId) { addToRemoveQueue(toastId) } else { state.toasts.forEach((toast) => { addToRemoveQueue(toast.id) }) } return { ...state, toasts: state.toasts.map((t) => t.id === toastId || toastId === undefined ? { ...t, open: false, } : t ), } } case "REMOVE_TOAST": if (action.toastId === undefined) { return { ...state, toasts: [], } } return { ...state, toasts: state.toasts.filter((t) => t.id !== action.toastId), } } } const listeners: Array<(state: State) => void> = [] let memoryState: State = { toasts: [] } function dispatch(action: Action) { memoryState = reducer(memoryState, action) listeners.forEach((listener) => { listener(memoryState) }) } type Toast = Omit<ToasterToast, "id"> function toast({ ...props }: Toast) { const id = genId() const update = (props: ToasterToast) => dispatch({ type: "UPDATE_TOAST", toast: { ...props, id }, }) const dismiss = () => dispatch({ type: "DISMISS_TOAST", toastId: id }) dispatch({ type: "ADD_TOAST", toast: { ...props, id, open: true, onOpenChange: (open) => { if (!open) dismiss() }, }, }) return { id: id, dismiss, update, } } function useToast() { const [state, setState] = React.useState<State>(memoryState) React.useEffect(() => { listeners.push(setState) return () => { const index = listeners.indexOf(setState) if (index > -1) { listeners.splice(index, 1) } } }, [state]) return { ...state, toast, dismiss: (toastId?: string) => dispatch({ type: "DISMISS_TOAST", toastId }), } } export { useToast, toast }
```

# lib\docling-processor.ts

```ts
// lib/docling-processor.ts import axios from 'axios'; import FormData from 'form-data'; export interface ProcessOptions { timeout?: number; } export interface ProcessResult { success: boolean; output: string; error?: string; } const PYTHON_API_URL = 'http://localhost:8000'; export class DoclingProcessor { public static async processDocument( filePath: string, options: ProcessOptions = {} ): Promise<ProcessResult> { try { // Create form data const formData = new FormData(); // Read the file as a Buffer const fs = await import('fs'); const fileBuffer = fs.readFileSync(filePath); // Append the file to form data formData.append('file', fileBuffer, { filename: filePath.split('/').pop() || 'document.pdf', contentType: 'application/pdf' }); // Set timeout const timeout = options.timeout || 300000; // 5 minutes default // Make request to Python API const response = await axios.post(`${PYTHON_API_URL}/process-pdf`, formData, { headers: { ...formData.getHeaders(), }, timeout: timeout, maxContentLength: Infinity, maxBodyLength: Infinity, }); if (response.status === 200) { return { success: true, output: JSON.stringify(response.data), }; } else { throw new Error(`API returned status ${response.status}`); } } catch (error) { console.error('Process document error:', error); return { success: false, output: '', error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error occurred', }; } } }
```

# lib\processors\document-processor.ts

```ts
import { writeFile } from 'fs/promises'; import path from 'path'; import { DoclingProcessor } from '../docling-processor'; export async function processDocument(file: File) { try { console.log('Processing document:', file.name); // Convert File to Buffer const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer(); const buffer = Buffer.from(arrayBuffer); // Create a safe filename with timestamp const timestamp = Date.now(); const safeFilename = `${timestamp}-${file.name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9.-]/g, '_')}`; // Save to public/uploads directory const uploadDir = path.join(process.cwd(), 'public', 'uploads'); const filePath = path.join(uploadDir, safeFilename); // Write file to disk await writeFile(filePath, buffer); // Process the document using DoclingProcessor const result = await DoclingProcessor.processDocument(filePath); if (!result.success) { throw new Error(result.error || 'Failed to process document'); } // Return in the format expected by test-document page return { text: result.output, metadata: { fileName: file.name, fileSize: file.size, format: path.extname(file.name).slice(1), processedAt: new Date().toISOString() } }; } catch (error) { console.error('Error processing document:', error); throw error; } }
```

```sql
-- CreateTable CREATE TABLE "Account" ( "id" TEXT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY, "userId" TEXT NOT NULL, "type" TEXT NOT NULL, "provider" TEXT NOT NULL, "providerAccountId" TEXT NOT NULL, "refresh_token" TEXT, "access_token" TEXT, "expires_at" INTEGER, "token_type" TEXT, "scope" TEXT, "id_token" TEXT, "session_state" TEXT, CONSTRAINT "Account_userId_fkey" FOREIGN KEY ("userId") REFERENCES "User" ("id") ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE ); # prisma\migrations\20241120171945_update_meetings_ownership.ts
```

```ts
// Nome do arquivo: prisma/migrations/[timestamp]_update_meetings_ownership.ts import { PrismaClient } from '@prisma/client'; const prisma = new PrismaClient(); async function main() { try { // Primeiro, vamos buscar o seu usuário (o primeiro usuário Google autenticado) const user = await prisma.user.findFirst({ where: { email: { contains: '@' // Isso pegará o primeiro usuário com email } } }); if (!user) { throw new Error('No user found! Please login first.'); } // Atualiza todas as reuniões para pertencerem ao seu usuário const updatedMeetings = await prisma.meeting.updateMany({ where: { userId: { equals: '' // Reuniões sem dono ou com userId vazio } }, data: { userId: user.id } }); console.log(`Updated ${updatedMeetings.count} meetings to user ${user.email}`); } catch (error) { console.error('Error updating meetings:', error); throw error; } } main() .catch((e) => { console.error(e); process.exit(1); }) .finally(async () => { await prisma.$disconnect(); });
```

# prisma\schema.prisma

```prisma
generator client { provider = "prisma-client-js" } datasource db { provider = "sqlite" url = "file:./dev.db" } model Account { id String @id @default(uuid()) userId String type String provider String providerAccountId String refresh_token String? access_token String? expires_at Int? token_type String? scope String? id_token String? session_state String? user User @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade) @@unique([provider, providerAccountId]) } model Session { id String @id @default(uuid()) sessionToken String @unique userId String expires DateTime user User @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade) } model User { id String @id @default(uuid()) name String? email String? @unique emailVerified DateTime? image String? accounts Account[] sessions Session[] } model VerificationToken { identifier String token String @unique expires DateTime @@unique([identifier, token]) } model Meeting { id String @id @default(uuid()) name String description String rawTranscript String // Raw transcript text summary String audioFile String? // URL or path to the audio file createdAt DateTime @default(now()) updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt userId String? // ID of the user who owns this meeting wordTimings String? // Store word-level timing information as stringified JSON speakerLabels String? // Store speaker diarization information as stringified JSON confidence Float? // Overall transcript confidence score language String? // Detected or specified language duration Float? // Audio duration in seconds fileSize Int? // Audio file size in bytes format String? // Audio file format tasks Task[] decisions Decision[] questions Question[] insights Insight[] deadlines Deadline[] attendees Attendee[] followUps FollowUp[] risks Risk[] agenda AgendaItem[] tags Tag[] comments Comment[] } model Task { id String @id @default(uuid()) task String owner String dueDate DateTime? priority String? // High, Medium, Low status String? // Not Started, In Progress, Completed assignee String? meetingId String createdAt DateTime @default(now()) updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt meeting Meeting @relation(fields: [meetingId], references: [id]) } model Decision { id String @id @default(uuid()) decision String date DateTime rationale String? impact String? approvedBy String? meetingId String createdAt DateTime @default(now()) updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt meeting Meeting @relation(fields: [meetingId], references: [id]) } model Question { id String @id @default(uuid()) question String status String // Asked, Answered, Deferred answer String? askedBy String? answeredBy String? meetingId String createdAt DateTime @default(now()) updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt meeting Meeting @relation(fields: [meetingId], references: [id]) } model Insight { id String @id @default(uuid()) insight String reference String category String? impact String? meetingId String createdAt DateTime @default(now()) updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt meeting Meeting @relation(fields: [meetingId], references: [id]) } model Deadline { id String @id @default(uuid()) description String dueDate DateTime? priority String? status String? meetingId String createdAt DateTime @default(now()) updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt meeting Meeting @relation(fields: [meetingId], references: [id]) } model Attendee { id String @id @default(uuid()) name String role String present Boolean? joinTime DateTime? leaveTime DateTime? meetingId String createdAt DateTime @default(now()) updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt meeting Meeting @relation(fields: [meetingId], references: [id]) } model FollowUp { id String @id @default(uuid()) description String owner String status String? dueDate DateTime? priority String? meetingId String createdAt DateTime @default(now()) updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt meeting Meeting @relation(fields: [meetingId], references: [id]) } model Risk { id String @id @default(uuid()) risk String impact String likelihood String? mitigation String? status String? meetingId String createdAt DateTime @default(now()) updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt meeting Meeting @relation(fields: [meetingId], references: [id]) } model AgendaItem { id String @id @default(uuid()) item String duration Int? presenter String? status String? notes String? meetingId String createdAt DateTime @default(now()) updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt meeting Meeting @relation(fields: [meetingId], references: [id]) } model Tag { id String @id @default(uuid()) name String @unique color String? description String? meetings Meeting[] createdAt DateTime @default(now()) updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt } model Comment { id String @id @default(uuid()) content String author String meetingId String createdAt DateTime @default(now()) updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt meeting Meeting @relation(fields: [meetingId], references: [id]) }
```

# python\server.py

```py
from fastapi import FastAPI, UploadFile, File, HTTPException
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
import uvicorn
import os
import fitz  # PyMuPDF
import traceback
from typing import Dict, Any
import shutil
from pathlib import Path

app = FastAPI()

# Configure CORS
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["http://localhost:3000"],
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

# Ensure upload directory exists
UPLOAD_DIR = Path("temp_uploads")
UPLOAD_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

def process_pdf_file(file_path: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """Process a PDF file and extract text and metadata."""
    doc = None
    try:
        # Open the PDF
        doc = fitz.open(file_path)
        
        # Extract text from all pages
        text = ""
        for page in doc:
            text += page.get_text()
            
        # Get metadata and page count before closing
        metadata = doc.metadata
        page_count = len(doc)
        
        return {
            "success": True,
            "text": text,
            "metadata": {
                "title": metadata.get("title", ""),
                "author": metadata.get("author", ""),
                "subject": metadata.get("subject", ""),
                "keywords": metadata.get("keywords", ""),
                "pageCount": page_count,
            }
        }
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error processing PDF: {str(e)}")
        print(traceback.format_exc())
        return {
            "success": False,
            "error": f"Failed to process PDF: {str(e)}"
        }
    finally:
        # Close the document in finally block
        if doc:
            doc.close()

@app.post("/process-pdf")
async def process_pdf(file: UploadFile = File(...)):
    if not file.filename.lower().endswith('.pdf'):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="File must be a PDF")

    print(f"Processing file: {file.filename}")
    
    # Create a unique filename
    temp_path = UPLOAD_DIR / f"temp_{file.filename}"
    try:
        # Save uploaded file
        print(f"Saving file to {temp_path}")
        with temp_path.open("wb") as buffer:
            shutil.copyfileobj(file.file, buffer)
        
        # Process the PDF
        result = process_pdf_file(str(temp_path))
        
        if not result["success"]:
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=500,
                detail=result["error"]
            )
            
        return result
            
    except Exception as e:
        print("Server error:", str(e))
        print(traceback.format_exc())
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=500,
            detail=f"Server error: {str(e)}"
        )
    finally:
        # Clean up temp file
        if temp_path.exists():
            print(f"Cleaning up {temp_path}")
            temp_path.unlink()

@app.on_event("startup")
async def startup_event():
    """Clear any leftover temporary files on startup"""
    if UPLOAD_DIR.exists():
        for file in UPLOAD_DIR.glob("temp_*"):
            try:
                file.unlink()
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"Failed to delete {file}: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    uvicorn.run(app, host="0.0.0.0", port=8000)

```

# README.md

```md
# Meeting Mind- An Hour Long Meeting Analyzed in Under 30 Seconds (Powered by Langflow) MeetingMind is an AI-powered meeting assistant that helps you capture, analyze, and act on your meeting insights effortlessly. This project is built with Langflow, Next.js and Groq-based fast transcription service to analyze your meetings and generate insights. ## Demo Check out this demo video to see MeetingMind in action: https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/50a9de7a-b24f-4167-9526-4e112b1d24f8 ## Features - Audio recording and file upload - AI-powered transcription - Automatic extraction of key information: - Tasks - Decisions - Questions - Insights - Deadlines - Attendees - Follow-ups - Risks - Agenda ## Getting Started ### Prerequisites - Node.js 14.x or later - npm or yarn - A LangFlow server running locally - Git (for cloning the repository) ### Caution ⚠️ **Important:** Groq Whisper used for transcription and analysis, currently supports files up to 25 MB only. There is a compression step in the process to reduce the file size to a manageable level. If your audio file is still larger than 25 MB, you will need to compress it before uploading. This limitation may affect the processing of longer meetings or high-quality audio recordings. To compress your audio files further, you can use tools like: - Online audio compressors - FFmpeg (command-line tool for audio/video processing) Ensure your compressed audio maintains sufficient quality for accurate transcription while staying under the 25 MB limit. ### Installation 1. Clone the repository: \`\`\`bash git clone https://github.com/yourusername/meetingmind.git cd meetingmind \`\`\` 2. Install dependencies: \`\`\`bash npm install # or yarn install \`\`\` 3. Set up LangFlow: - Install and run the LangFlow backend server - Upload the flow provided in the repo at `utils/langflow_flow/Meeting Mind.json` - Note the URL of your LangFlow server 4. Create a `.env.local` file in the root directory and add the LangFlow URL: \`\`\` LANGFLOW_FLOW_URL="http://127.0.0.1:7860/api/v1/run/5781a690-e689-4b26-b636-45da76a91915" \`\`\` Replace the URL with your actual LangFlow server URL if different. In the file `app/api/transcribe/route.ts`, locate the `payload` object and update the Groq component name to match your LangFlow component name. For example: \`\`\`typescript const payload = { output_type: 'text', input_type: 'text', tweaks: { 'YourGroqComponentName': { audio_file: filePath }, } } \`\`\` Replace 'YourGroqComponentName' with the actual name of your Groq component in LangFlow. 5. Set up the database: This project uses Prisma as an ORM. By default, it's configured to use SQLite as the database. a. To use the local SQLite database: - Ensure your `.env` file contains: \`\`\` DATABASE_URL="file:./dev.db" \`\`\` - Run the following commands to set up your database: \`\`\`bash npx prisma generate npx prisma migrate dev --name init \`\`\` b. To use a different database (e.g., PostgreSQL with Neon): - Update your `.env` file with the appropriate connection string: \`\`\` DATABASE_URL="postgresql://username:password@host:port/database?schema=public" \`\`\` - Update the `provider` in `prisma/schema.prisma`: \`\`\`prisma datasource db { provider = "postgresql" url = env("DATABASE_URL") } \`\`\` - Run the Prisma commands as mentioned above to generate the client and run migrations. 6. Run the development server: \`\`\`bash npm run dev # or yarn dev \`\`\` 7. Open [http://localhost:3000](http://localhost:3000) with your browser to see the result. ## Usage 1. Navigate to the dashboard page. 2. Upload an audio file. 3. Wait for the AI to process and analyze the meeting. 4. Review the extracted information in the Dashboard. ## Project Structure - `app/`: Contains the main application code - `components/`: Reusable React components - `api/`: API routes for server-side functionality - `dashboard/`: Dashboard page component - `page.tsx`: Home page component - `public/`: Static assets - `prisma/`: Database schema and migrations - `utils/`: Utility functions and configurations - `lib/`: Shared libraries and modules ## Technologies Used - Langflow: For AI workflow management - Next.js: React framework for building the web application - React: JavaScript library for building user interfaces - Tailwind CSS: Utility-first CSS framework - Framer Motion: Animation library for React - Axios: Promise-based HTTP client - Prisma: ORM for database management - SQLite: Default database (can be changed to PostgreSQL or others) - Groq: AI model provider for transcription and analysis ## Configuration - The project uses environment variables for configuration. Ensure all necessary variables are set in your `.env.local` file. - Tailwind CSS configuration can be found in `tailwind.config.ts`. - TypeScript configuration is in `tsconfig.json`. ## API Routes - `/api/meetings`: Handles CRUD operations for meetings - `/api/transcribe`: Handles audio file transcription and analysis ## Debugging - Use the browser's developer tools to debug client-side issues. - For server-side debugging, use console.log statements or attach a debugger to your Node.js process. ## Performance Considerations - Large audio files may take longer to process. Consider implementing a progress indicator for better user experience. - Optimize database queries and indexes for improved performance as the number of meetings grows. ## Screenshots ### Landing Page ![Landing Page](public/landing.webp) ### Dashboard ![Dashboard](public/dashboard.png) #### Meeting Summary ![Meeting Summary](public/meeting_summary.png) #### Meeting Details ![Meeting Details](public/meeting_details.png) These screenshots provide a visual representation of the application's main interfaces. The landing page showcases the initial user experience, while the dashboard displays the core functionality where users can upload audio files and view the AI-processed meeting information. ## Contributing Contributions are welcome! Please feel free to submit a Pull Request. Here are some ways you can contribute: - Report bugs and issues - Suggest new features - Improve documentation - Submit pull requests with bug fixes or new features Please read our contributing guidelines before submitting a pull request. ## License This project is licensed under the MIT License. See the LICENSE file for details. ## Support If you encounter any problems or have questions, please open an issue on the GitHub repository. ## Acknowledgements - Thanks to the Langflow team for providing the AI workflow management tool. - Special thanks to all contributors who have helped shape this project.
```

# scripts\fix-transcripts.js

```js
const { PrismaClient } = require('@prisma/client'); const prisma = new PrismaClient(); async function fixTranscripts() { try { // Get all meetings const meetings = await prisma.meeting.findMany(); for (const meeting of meetings) { try { let text = meeting.rawTranscript; // Only try to parse if it looks like JSON if (meeting.rawTranscript.startsWith('{')) { const parsed = JSON.parse(meeting.rawTranscript); // Check if it's the old format with full transcription object if (parsed.text) { text = parsed.text; } // If it's already just text in JSON format, leave it as is } // If it's not JSON, assume it's already plain text // Update only if the format needs to be changed if (text !== meeting.rawTranscript) { await prisma.meeting.update({ where: { id: meeting.id }, data: { rawTranscript: text } }); console.log(`Updated meeting ${meeting.id}`); } else { console.log(`Meeting ${meeting.id} already in correct format`); } } catch (e) { console.error(`Failed to update meeting ${meeting.id}:`, e); } } console.log('Finished updating meetings'); } catch (e) { console.error('Failed to fix transcripts:', e); } finally { await prisma.$disconnect(); } } fixTranscripts();
```

# scripts\fix-transcripts.ts

```ts
import { prisma } from '../lib/prisma'; async function fixTranscripts() { try { // Get all meetings const meetings = await prisma.meeting.findMany(); for (const meeting of meetings) { try { let text = meeting.rawTranscript; // Only try to parse if it looks like JSON if (meeting.rawTranscript.startsWith('{')) { const parsed = JSON.parse(meeting.rawTranscript); // Check if it's the old format with full transcription object if (parsed.text) { text = parsed.text; } // If it's already just text in JSON format, leave it as is } // If it's not JSON, assume it's already plain text // Update only if the format needs to be changed if (text !== meeting.rawTranscript) { await prisma.meeting.update({ where: { id: meeting.id }, data: { rawTranscript: text } }); console.log(`Updated meeting ${meeting.id}`); } else { console.log(`Meeting ${meeting.id} already in correct format`); } } catch (e) { console.error(`Failed to update meeting ${meeting.id}:`, e); } } console.log('Finished updating meetings'); } catch (e) { console.error('Failed to fix transcripts:', e); } finally { await prisma.$disconnect(); } } fixTranscripts();
```

# scripts\retranscribe-meetings.js

```js
const { PrismaClient } = require('@prisma/client'); const prisma = new PrismaClient(); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path'); const axios = require('axios'); // ... (Existing createSegmentsFromWords and parseTranscriptionResponse functions from app/api/transcribe/route.ts) async function retranscribeMeetings() { try { const meetings = await prisma.meeting.findMany(); for (const meeting of meetings) { try { // Skip if rawTranscript is already plain text if (!meeting.rawTranscript.startsWith('{')) { console.log(`Meeting ${meeting.id} already in correct format, skipping`); continue; } const audioFilePath = path.join(process.cwd(), 'public', meeting.audioFile); if (!fs.existsSync(audioFilePath)) { console.error(`Audio file not found for meeting ${meeting.id}: ${audioFilePath}`); continue; } console.log(`Retranscribing meeting ${meeting.id} from ${audioFilePath}`); // Simulate file upload for the transcription process const fileContent = fs.readFileSync(audioFilePath); const fileName = meeting.audioFile.split('/').pop(); // Extract filename from URL const file = new File([fileContent], fileName, { type: 'audio/mpeg' }); // Adjust type if needed const apiUrl = process.env.LANGFLOW_FLOW_URL; if (!apiUrl) { throw new Error('LANGFLOW_FLOW_URL is not defined'); } const payload = { output_type: 'text', input_type: 'text', tweaks: { 'GroqWhisperComponent-Y7ZzR': { audio_file: audioFilePath, // Use the actual file path }, }, }; const apiResponse = await axios.post(apiUrl, payload, { headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', }, }); const outputs = apiResponse.data.outputs; const transcriptionResult = outputs[0]?.outputs[1]?.results?.transcription; if (!transcriptionResult) { throw new Error('Missing transcript data'); } const parsedTranscription = parseTranscriptionResponse(transcriptionResult); await prisma.meeting.update({ where: { id: meeting.id }, data: { rawTranscript: parsedTranscription.text, wordTimings: JSON.stringify(parsedTranscription.word_timestamps), segments: JSON.stringify(parsedTranscription.segments), // Store segments }, }); console.log(`Updated meeting ${meeting.id}`); } catch (e) { console.error(`Failed to retranscribe meeting ${meeting.id}:`, e); } } console.log('Finished retranscribing meetings'); } catch (e) { console.error('Failed to retranscribe meetings:', e); } finally { await prisma.$disconnect(); } } retranscribeMeetings();
```

# types\global.d.ts

```ts
/// <reference types="react" /> declare global { namespace JSX { interface IntrinsicElements { [elemName: string]: any; } } } export interface Meeting { id: string; name: string; description: string; rawTranscript: string; summary: string; audioFile: string | null; createdAt: Date; updatedAt: Date; wordTimings: string | null; speakerLabels: string | null; confidence: number | null; language: string | null; duration: number | null; fileSize: number | null; format: string | null; tasks: Task[]; decisions: Decision[]; questions: Question[]; insights: Insight[]; deadlines: Deadline[]; attendees: Attendee[]; followUps: FollowUp[]; risks: Risk[]; agenda: AgendaItem[]; } export interface Task { id: string; task: string; owner: string; dueDate: Date | null; priority?: string | null; status?: string | null; assignee?: string | null; meetingId: string; createdAt: Date; updatedAt: Date; } export interface Decision { id: string; decision: string; date: Date; rationale?: string | null; impact?: string | null; approvedBy?: string | null; meetingId: string; createdAt: Date; updatedAt: Date; } export interface Question { id: string; question: string; status: string; answer: string | null; askedBy?: string | null; answeredBy?: string | null; meetingId: string; createdAt: Date; updatedAt: Date; } export interface Insight { id: string; insight: string; reference: string; category?: string | null; impact?: string | null; meetingId: string; createdAt: Date; updatedAt: Date; } export interface Deadline { id: string; description: string; dueDate: Date | null; priority?: string | null; status?: string | null; meetingId: string; createdAt: Date; updatedAt: Date; } export interface Attendee { id: string; name: string; role: string; present?: boolean | null; joinTime?: Date | null; leaveTime?: Date | null; meetingId: string; createdAt: Date; updatedAt: Date; } export interface FollowUp { id: string; description: string; owner: string; status?: string | null; dueDate?: Date | null; priority?: string | null; meetingId: string; createdAt: Date; updatedAt: Date; } export interface Risk { id: string; risk: string; impact: string; likelihood?: string | null; mitigation?: string | null; status?: string | null; meetingId: string; createdAt: Date; updatedAt: Date; } export interface AgendaItem { id: string; item: string; duration?: number | null; presenter?: string | null; status?: string | null; notes?: string | null; meetingId: string; createdAt: Date; updatedAt: Date; } export interface WordTiming { word: string; start: number; end: number; confidence: number; speaker_id?: string; punctuated?: boolean; language_code?: string; } export interface SpeakerLabel { speaker: string; start: number; end: number; confidence: number; speaker_id: string; channel?: number; gender?: string; } export interface TranscriptSegment { text: string; start: number; end: number; speaker: string; words: WordTiming[]; } export interface MeetingBreakdown { Tasks: { task: string; owner: string; due_date: Date | null; }[]; Decisions: { decision: string; date: Date; }[]; Questions: { question: string; status: string; answer: string | null; }[]; Insights: { insight: string; reference: string; }[]; Deadlines: { description: string; due_date: Date | null; }[]; Attendees: { name: string; role: string; }[]; "Follow-ups": { description: string; owner: string; }[]; Risks: { risk: string; impact: string; }[]; Agenda: { item: string; }[]; } export interface MeetingWithParsedFields extends Omit<Meeting, 'wordTimings' | 'speakerLabels'> { wordTimings: WordTiming[] | null; segments: TranscriptSegment[] | null; speakerLabels: SpeakerLabel[] | null; breakdown: MeetingBreakdown; } export interface TranscriptionResponse { outputs: Array<{ outputs: Array<{ results?: { breakdown?: { text: string; }; transcription?: { text: string; word_timestamps?: WordTiming[]; speaker_labels?: SpeakerLabel[]; segments?: TranscriptSegment[]; }; }; }>; }>; }
```
